<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Dawn_Era">Dawn Era</span></h2>
<ul><li>The brothers <a href="/wiki/Anu" title="Anu">Anu</a> and <a href="/wiki/Padomay" title="Padomay">Padomay</a> enter into the <a href="/wiki/Void" title="Void">Void</a>, and time begins.
</li><li>They give birth to their own Souls, <a href="/wiki/Anui-El" title="Anui-El">Anui-El</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sithis_(Deity)" title="Sithis (Deity)">Sithis</a>, whose interplay creates the <a href="/wiki/Aurbis" title="Aurbis">Aurbis</a>.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Lorkhan" title="Lorkhan">Lorkhan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Auriel" title="Auriel" class="mw-redirect">Auriel</a> are the first spirits born into the Aurbis, Lorkhan wanders and Auriel creates time.
</li><li>The Original Spirits or <a href="/wiki/Et%27Ada" title="Et'Ada">et'Ada</a> emerge within the Aurbis are either aligned with Anu (Anuic spirits) or Padomay (Padomaic spirits).
</li><li>Lorkhan, a Padomaic spirit, travels the Aurbis and conceives the concept that <a href="/wiki/Mundus" title="Mundus">Mundus</a> should be created.
</li><li>Lorkhan then tricks/convinces other et'Ada to join him. Those that do become the <a href="/wiki/Aedra" title="Aedra">Aedra</a> and those that don't become the <a href="/wiki/Daedra" title="Daedra">Daedra</a>.
</li><li>The Aedra create 12 worlds of creation. Some creation myths believe each world is a God. These 12 worlds are molded together to create <a href="/wiki/Nirn" title="Nirn">Nirn</a>.
</li><li>Many of the Aedra die during the creation with some becoming mortals to ensure the continuation of life on Mundus whilst some become the <a href="/wiki/Ehlnofey" title="Ehlnofey">Ehlnofey</a> or "Earthbones," the Laws of Nature.
</li><li>Many of the Aedra flee back to <a href="/wiki/Aetherius" title="Aetherius">Aetherius</a>, which is a part of Aurbis, and become the Magne-ge, tearing holes in Oblivion.
</li><li>Auri-El establishes the first kingdoms of the Old Ehlnofey on <a href="/wiki/Atmora" title="Atmora">Atmora</a> and the supposed land <a href="/wiki/Aldmeris" title="Aldmeris">Aldmeris</a>. These lands are where the <a href="/wiki/Aldmer" title="Aldmer">Aldmer</a> originate.
</li><li>A large number of Aedra are disappointed and angry with the creation of Mundus and seek revenge. These include the ancestors of Elves - the Old Ehlnofey, whose leader was <a href="/wiki/Auri-El" title="Auri-El">Auri-El</a> and whose heroes included <a href="/wiki/Trinimac" title="Trinimac">Trinimac</a>, <a href="/wiki/Phynaster_(Deity)" title="Phynaster (Deity)">Phynaster</a> and <a href="/wiki/Syrabane" title="Syrabane">Syrabane</a>.
</li><li>Auri-El sought out Lorkhan in battle and warred with him. Lorkhan's followers included the ancestors of Man—the Wandering Ehlnofey and whose heroes included <a href="/wiki/Kyne" title="Kyne">Kyne</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tsun" title="Tsun">Tsun</a>, <a href="/wiki/Stuhn" title="Stuhn">Stuhn</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jhunal" title="Jhunal">Jhunal</a>.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Atmora" title="Atmora">Atmora</a> is conquered by the armies of man.
</li><li>The great war ends when Trinimac tears Lorkhan's heart out and Auri-El fires it into the sea with his bow.
</li><li>The war causes the mega-continent on Nirn to become flooded and fracture into smaller continents and islands.
</li><li>The lands inhabited by the Wandering Ehlnofey, which include <a href="/wiki/Akavir_(Continent)" title="Akavir (Continent)">Akavir</a>, <a href="/wiki/Atmora" title="Atmora">Atmora</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Yokuda" title="Yokuda">Yokuda</a>, become isolated. These lands are where the <a href="/wiki/Tsaesci" title="Tsaesci">Tsaesci</a>, <a href="/wiki/Atmoran" title="Atmoran">Atmorans</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yokudan" title="Yokudan" class="mw-redirect">Yokudans</a> originate.
</li><li>Some Wandering Ehlnofey remain on <a href="/wiki/Tamriel" title="Tamriel">Tamriel</a>, they become the <a href="/wiki/Nede" title="Nede">Nedes</a>.
</li><li>The Old Ehlnofey remain on the supposed land <a href="/wiki/Aldmeris" title="Aldmeris">Aldmeris</a> and become the <a href="/wiki/Aldmer" title="Aldmer">Aldmer</a>.
</li></ul>
<p>Sources: <i><a href="/wiki/The_Monomyth" title="The Monomyth">The Monomyth</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Annotated_Anuad" title="The Annotated Anuad">The Annotated Anuad</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Vehk%27s_Teaching" title="Vehk's Teaching">Vehk's Teaching</a></i>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merethic_Era">Merethic Era</span></h2>
<p><b>Merethic timeline provided by the Imperial Library</b>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Circa_ME_2500">Circa ME 2500</span></h4>
<ul><li>Supposed date of construction of the <a href="/wiki/Direnni_Tower" title="Direnni Tower">Adamantine Tower</a> (also known as the <a href="/wiki/Direnni_Tower" title="Direnni Tower">Direnni Tower</a>) on <a href="/wiki/Balfiera" title="Balfiera" class="mw-redirect">Balfiera Island</a> in <a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a>, the oldest known structure of <a href="/wiki/Tamriel" title="Tamriel">Tamriel</a>. Earliest historical date in unpublished Elvish chronicles.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:HR_0-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:HR-0">[1]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Merethic_Era">Early Merethic Era</span></h4>
<ul><li>Aboriginal beastpeoples (ancestors of the <a href="/wiki/Khajiit" title="Khajiit">Khajiit</a>, <a href="/wiki/Argonian" title="Argonian">Argonian</a>, and other beastfolk) live in preliterate communities throughout Tamriel.
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Middle_Merethic_Era">Middle Merethic Era</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Aldmer" title="Aldmer">Aldmer</a> leave the supposed doomed and now-lost continent of <a href="/wiki/Aldmeris" title="Aldmeris">Aldmeris</a> (also known as 'Old Ehlnofey') and settle in Tamriel. First colonies are distributed widely along the entire coast of Tamriel. Later, inland settlements were founded primarily in fertile lowlands in southwest and central Tamriel.
</li><li>The sophisticated, literate, and technologically advanced Aldmeri culture drove the primitive <a href="/wiki/Beastfolk" title="Beastfolk">beastfolk</a> into the jungles, marshes, mountains, and wastelands.
</li><li>The Adamantine Tower is rediscovered and captured by the <a href="/wiki/Direnni_Bloodline" title="Direnni Bloodline">Direnni</a>, a prominent and powerful Aldmeri clan. <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Tower_(Location)" title="Crystal Tower (Location)">Crystal Tower</a> is built on <a href="/wiki/Summerset_Isle" title="Summerset Isle" class="mw-redirect">Summerset Isle</a> and, later, <a href="/wiki/White-Gold_Tower" title="White-Gold Tower">White-Gold Tower</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cyrodiil" title="Cyrodiil">Cyrodiil</a>.
</li><li>One of these Aldmeri Explorers, <a href="/wiki/Torval_the_Pilot" title="Torval the Pilot" class="mw-redirect">Torval the Pilot</a>, explores and charts Tamriel sea-lanes and the <a href="/wiki/Niben_River" title="Niben River">River Niben</a>, located in southern Tamriel. He sails deep into central Cyrodiil, and acquires the Eight Islands (the site of White Gold Tower) from the beastfolk natives for the secret of literacy.
</li><li>Aldmeri explorers map the coasts of <a href="/wiki/Vvardenfell" title="Vvardenfell">Vvardenfell</a>, building the First Era High Elven wizard towers at Ald Redaynia, Bal Fell, Tel Aruhn, and Tel Mora in <a href="/wiki/Morrowind" title="Morrowind">Morrowind</a>.
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Ayleid" title="Ayleid">Ayleids</a> flourish in the jungles surrounding White Gold Tower (present day Cyrodiil). Ayleids, also known as the Heartland High Elves, preserved the Dawn Era magicks and language of the Ehlnofey.
</li><li>Ostensibly a tribute-land to the High King of <a href="/wiki/Alinor" title="Alinor">Alinor</a>, Cyrodiil was often so isolated from the Summerset Isles as to be its own sovereign nation.
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Late_Middle_Merethic_Era">Late Middle Merethic Era</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Dwemer" title="Dwemer">Dwemer</a>, a free-thinking, reclusive Elven clan devoted to the secrets of science, engineering, and alchemy, established underground cities and communities in the mountain range (later the <a href="/wiki/Velothi_Mountains" title="Velothi Mountains">Velothi Mountains</a>) separating modern Skyrim and Resdayn/Morrowind.
</li><li>The Late Middle Merethic Era is also the period of the High Velothi Culture.
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Chimer" title="Chimer">Chimer</a> (ancestors of the modern <a href="/wiki/Dunmer" title="Dunmer">Dunmer</a>, or Dark Elves), dynamic, ambitious, long-lived Elven clans devoted to fundamentalist ancestor worship, followed the Prophet <a href="/wiki/Veloth" title="Veloth">Veloth</a> out of ancestral Elven homelands to settle in the lands now known as Morrowind.
</li><li>Despising the secular culture and profane practices of the Dwemer, the Chimer also coveted the lands and resources of the Dwemer, and for centuries provoked them with minor raids and territorial disputes.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Trinimac" title="Trinimac">Trinimac</a> (strongest of the Altmeri ancestor spirits) and his people (who became the <a href="/wiki/Orsimer" title="Orsimer">Orsimer</a> or the Pariah Folk) try to halt Velothi dissident movement. However, Daedric Prince <a href="/wiki/Boethiah" title="Boethiah">Boethiah</a>, as one of the masterminds of the movement, eats Trinimac. Trinimac's body and spirit are corrupted, and he emerges as Daedric Prince <a href="/wiki/Malacath" title="Malacath">Malacath</a>. The rest of his people are changed as well. They are now known as Orcs.
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Late_Merethic_Era">Late Merethic Era</span></h4>
<ul><li>Velothi high culture disappears on Vvardenfell Island. The earliest Dwemer Freehold colonies date from this period.
</li><li>Degenerate Velothi devolves into tribal cultures, which, in time, evolves into the modern Great Houses of Morrowind, or persists as the barbarian <a href="/wiki/Ashlander" title="Ashlander">Ashlander</a> tribes. The only surviving traces of this tribal culture are scattered Velothi towers and Ashlander nomads on Vvardenfell Island. The original First Era High Elven wizard towers along the coasts of Tamriel are also abandoned about this time.
</li><li>The proto-Nords in the final migration from <a href="/wiki/Atmora" title="Atmora">Atmora</a> (also known as 'Altmora' or 'the Elder Wood' in <a href="/wiki/Aldmeris" title="Aldmeris">Aldmeris</a>) settle in northern Tamriel. Nordic hero <a href="/wiki/Ysgramor_(Lore)" title="Ysgramor (Lore)" class="mw-redirect">Ysgramor</a>, leader of a great colonizing fleet to Tamriel, develops a runic transcription of Nordic speech based on Elvish principles, and is the first human historian.
</li><li>Ysgramor's fleet lands at <a href="/wiki/Hsaarik_Head" title="Hsaarik Head">Hsaarik Head</a> at the extreme northern tip of Skyrim's Broken Cape.
</li><li>The Nords build there the legendary city of <a href="/wiki/Saarthal" title="Saarthal">Saarthal</a>.
</li><li>The Elves drive the Men away during the <a href="/wiki/Night_of_Tears" title="Night of Tears">Night of Tears</a>, but Ysgramor soon returns with his Five Hundred Companions.
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Late_Merethic_Era_-_Circa_1E_660">Late Merethic Era - Circa 1E 660</span></h4>
<ul><li>An immortal hero, warrior, sorcerer, and king variously known as <a href="/wiki/Pelinal_Whitestrake" title="Pelinal Whitestrake">Pelinal Whitestrake</a>, Harrald Hairy Breeks, Ysmir, <a href="/wiki/Wulfharth" title="Wulfharth">Wulfharth</a>, Hans the Fox, etc., wanders Tamriel, gathering armies, conquering lands, ruling, then abandoning his kingdoms to wander again.
</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="First_Era">First Era</span></h2>
<p><b>Undetermined date/works in progress</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Daggerfall" title="Daggerfall">Daggerfall</a> defeats the <a href="/wiki/Akaviri_Invasion" title="Akaviri Invasion" class="mw-redirect">Akaviri Invasion</a> ("If Daggerfall had not spent its first thousand years preparing for the battles of the next thousand years, it is indeed conceivable that the Iliac Bay today might be <a href="/wiki/Akaviri" title="Akaviri">Akaviri</a>.")<sup id="cite_ref-AHoD_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AHoD-1">[2]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1st_Century">1st Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_0">1E 0</span></h4>
<ul><li>King <a href="/wiki/Eplear" title="Eplear">Eplear</a> begins the <a href="/wiki/First_Era" title="First Era">First Era</a> by founding the <a href="/wiki/Camoran_Dynasty" title="Camoran Dynasty">Camoran Dynasty</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:V_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:V-3">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[5]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_20">1E 20</span></h4>
<ul><li>The earliest recordings of the <a href="/wiki/Psijic_Order" title="Psijic Order">Psijic Order</a> is recorded, telling the tale of the renowned Breton sage and author Voernet, traveling to the Isle of Artaeum to meet with <a href="/wiki/Iachesis" title="Iachesis">Iachesis</a>, the Ritemaster of the Psijics.<sup id="cite_ref-Fragment_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fragment-5">[6]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_68">1E 68</span></h4>
<ul><li>The last visit from <a href="/wiki/Atmora" title="Atmora">Atmora</a> to <a href="/wiki/Tamriel" title="Tamriel">Tamriel</a> occurs: two ships, largely laden with corpses.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[7]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2nd_Century">2nd Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_113">1E 113</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Harald" title="Harald">Harald</a> is born. He later becomes the first Nordic ruler.<sup id="cite_ref-Frontier_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Frontier-7">[8]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:C_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:C-8">[9]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_139">1E 139</span></h4>
<ul><li>King <a href="/wiki/Harald" title="Harald">Harald</a> orders a campaign against the remaining <a href="/wiki/Snow_Elves" title="Snow Elves" class="mw-redirect">Snow Elves</a> in the region near <a href="/wiki/Lake_Honrich" title="Lake Honrich">Lake Honrich</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Skorm_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Skorm-9">[10]</a></sup>
</li><li>One of the last remnants of the <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Cult" title="Dragon Cult">Dragon Cult</a> is discovered in the secluded monastery of <a href="/wiki/Forelhost" title="Forelhost">Forelhost</a> by one of King Harald's armies.<sup id="cite_ref-Skorm_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Skorm-9">[10]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_140">1E 140</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Skorm_Snow-Strider" title="Skorm Snow-Strider">Skorm Snow-Strider</a> finds Forelhost devoid of life, the cultists previously inhabiting the fortress having slit their own wrists or been poisoned. He loses half his men to poisoned water found within the monastery.<sup id="cite_ref-Skorm_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Skorm-9">[10]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_143">1E 143</span></h4>
<ul><li>King <a href="/wiki/Harald" title="Harald">Harald</a> conquers Skyrim.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_198">1E 198</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Scouring_of_Wendelbeck?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Scouring of Wendelbeck (page does not exist)">Scouring of Wendelbeck</a>, a battle during the <a href="/wiki/Narfinsel_Schism" title="Narfinsel Schism">Narfinsel Schism</a>, occurs, marking the war's climax.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[12]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="3rd_Century">3rd Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_200">1E 200</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Tamrilean_Tractates" title="Tamrilean Tractates">Tamrilean Tractates</a> are written.<sup id="cite_ref-HTON_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HTON-12">[13]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_221">1E 221</span></h4>
<ul><li>King <a href="/wiki/Harald" title="Harald">Harald</a> dies at 108 years of age.<sup id="cite_ref-Frontier_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Frontier-7">[8]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Moot" title="Moot">Moot</a> is created.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:S_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:S-13">[14]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Hjalmer" title="Hjalmer">Hjalmer</a>, the son of King Harald, takes his throne.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_221.2B">1E 221+</span></h4>
<ul><li>In the years following King Harald's death, <a href="/wiki/Dwemer" title="Dwemer">Dwemer</a> of Skyrim discovered a considerable source of raw <a href="/wiki/Aetherium" title="Aetherium">Aetherium</a> in <a href="/wiki/Blackreach" title="Blackreach">Blackreach</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-aether_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-aether-14">[15]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-kat_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-kat-15">[16]</a></sup>
</li><li>An alliance between four <a href="/wiki/Dwemer" title="Dwemer">Dwemer</a> cities of <a href="/wiki/Arkngthamz" title="Arkngthamz">Arkngthamz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Raldbthar" title="Raldbthar">Raldbthar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mzulft" title="Mzulft">Mzulft</a>, and Bthar-zel (now known as <a href="/wiki/Deep_Folk_Crossing" title="Deep Folk Crossing">Deep Folk Crossing</a>) is created to oversee the extraction, processing, and study of <a href="/wiki/Aetherium" title="Aetherium">Aetherium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-aether_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-aether-14">[15]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Dwemer construct the <a href="/wiki/Aetherium_Forge" title="Aetherium Forge">Aetherium Forge</a> under the city of <a href="/wiki/Ruins_of_Bthalft" title="Ruins of Bthalft">Bthalft</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-aether_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-aether-14">[15]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Aetherium_Wars" title="Aetherium Wars">Aetherium Wars</a> take place between the Dwemer city states of Skyrim. It lasts for several decades.<sup id="cite_ref-aether_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-aether-14">[15]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_222">1E 222</span></h4>
<ul><li>King <a href="/wiki/Hjalmer" title="Hjalmer">Hjalmer</a> dies.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li><li>Rule of Nordic <a href="/wiki/High_King" title="High King">High King</a> <a href="/wiki/Vrage" title="Vrage">Vrage</a> the Gifted begins, right after the death of <a href="/wiki/Hjalmer" title="Hjalmer">Hjalmer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:S_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:S-13">[14]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[17]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_227">1E 227</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Gradual_Massacre?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Gradual Massacre (page does not exist)">Gradual Massacre</a> begins.<sup id="cite_ref-HTON_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HTON-12">[13]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_240">1E 240</span></h4>
<ul><li>King <a href="/wiki/Vrage" title="Vrage">Vrage</a> begins the <a href="/wiki/Skyrim_Conquests" title="Skyrim Conquests">Skyrim Conquests</a>, which involves the annexation of <a href="/wiki/Morrowind" title="Morrowind">Morrowind</a> and <a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LCST_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LCST-17">[18]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:HR_0-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:HR-0">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:M_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:M-18">[19]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:M_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:M-19">[20]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_240.2B">1E 240+</span></h4>
<ul><li>At some point after 1E 240, King <a href="/wiki/Gellir" title="Gellir">Gellir</a> becomes High King of Skyrim and conquers the weakened Dwemer city states across the land.<sup id="cite_ref-aether_14-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-aether-14">[15]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_242">1E 242</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Alessia" title="Alessia">Alessia</a>, her demigod lover, Morihaus-Breath-of-Kyne, and Pelinal Whitestrake, start the <a href="/wiki/Cyrodiil" title="Cyrodiil">Cyrodiilic</a> human uprising against the <a href="/wiki/Ayleid" title="Ayleid">Ayleid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:C_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:C-20">[21]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Shezzar_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shezzar-21">[22]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LKoA_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LKoA-22">[23]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_243">1E 243</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/White-Gold_Tower" title="White-Gold Tower">White-Gold Tower</a> falls. This is seen as the symbolic end of the <a href="/wiki/Ayleid" title="Ayleid">Ayleid</a> Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Shezzar_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shezzar-21">[22]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LKoA_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LKoA-22">[23]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Alessian_Empire" title="Alessian Empire">Alessian Empire</a> of <a href="/wiki/Cyrodiil" title="Cyrodiil">Cyrodiil</a> is officially formed. (The "First Empire")<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:V_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:V-3">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:C_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:C-8">[9]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:E_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:E-23">[24]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:BM_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:BM-24">[25]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_246">1E 246</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Daggerfall" title="Daggerfall">Daggerfall</a> is founded as the capital in <a href="/wiki/Iliac_Bay" title="Iliac Bay">Iliac Bay</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-AHoD_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AHoD-1">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BethsoftTimeline_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BethsoftTimeline-25">[OOG 1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_263">1E 263</span></h4>
<ul><li>Several <a href="/wiki/Ayleid" title="Ayleid">Ayleid</a> princes continue to rule, as vassals of the new Empress. From here until <a href="#1E_498">1E 498</a>, Ayleids would continue to have minor influence, in what can be called the "Late Ayleid Period."<sup id="cite_ref-LKoA_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LKoA-22">[23]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_266">1E 266</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Apotheosis_(Term)" title="Apotheosis (Term)">Apotheosis</a> of <a href="/wiki/Alessia" title="Alessia">Alessia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Cleansing_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cleansing-26">[26]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Alessia" title="Alessia">Alessian</a> articles and Calendars begin from this year.<sup id="cite_ref-Cleansing_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cleansing-26">[26]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Belharza_the_Man-Bull" title="Belharza the Man-Bull" class="mw-redirect">Belharza the Man-Bull</a> becomes the Second Emperor of the <a href="/wiki/Alessian_Empire" title="Alessian Empire">Alessian Empire</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Cleansing_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cleansing-26">[26]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="4th_Century">4th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_340">1E 340</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Bosmer" title="Bosmer">Bosmer</a> <a href="/wiki/Camoran_Dynasty" title="Camoran Dynasty">Camoran Dynasty</a> of <a href="/wiki/Valenwood" title="Valenwood">Valenwood</a> forms a treaty with the <a href="/wiki/Alessian_Order" title="Alessian Order">Alessian Order</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:V_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:V-3">[4]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_355">1E 355</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Clan_Direnni" title="Clan Direnni" class="mw-redirect">Clan Direnni</a> rises to power in <a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_358">1E 358</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Direnni_Hegemony" title="Direnni Hegemony">Direnni Hegemony</a> occurs, during which Skyrim loses significant amounts of land to the Direnni.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_361">1E 361</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Alessia" title="Alessia">Alessians</a> gain control of the Empire, and enforce the <a href="/wiki/Alessian_Doctrines" title="Alessian Doctrines">Alessian Doctrines</a> of <a href="/wiki/Marukh" title="Marukh">Marukh</a> throughout the Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-LKoA_22-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LKoA-22">[23]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li>Ayleid lordships are outlawed.<sup id="cite_ref-LKoA_22-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LKoA-22">[23]</a></sup>
</li><li>Little resistance to this, and so most Ayleids simply left Cyrodiil, and many are absorbed into the native population of Elves in <a href="/wiki/Valenwood" title="Valenwood">Valenwood</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-LKoA_22-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LKoA-22">[23]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_369">1E 369</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Wild_Hunt" title="Wild Hunt">Wild Hunt</a> takes place, and King <a href="/wiki/Borgas" title="Borgas">Borgas</a> of <a href="/wiki/Winterhold_(Hold)" title="Winterhold (Hold)">Winterhold</a> is killed.<sup id="cite_ref-AHoD_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AHoD-1">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:C_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:C-8">[9]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:S_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:S-13">[14]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:AD_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:AD-28">[28]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/War_of_Succession" title="War of Succession">War of Succession</a> begins.<sup id="cite_ref-AHoD_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AHoD-1">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:C_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:C-8">[9]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:AD_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:AD-28">[28]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Skyrim" title="Skyrim">Skyrim</a> begins to lose its holdings in <a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a> and <a href="/wiki/Morrowind" title="Morrowind">Morrowind</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:C_8-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:C-8">[9]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_376">1E 376</span></h4>
<ul><li>The traditional rule of Yokuda's emperors is overthrown. Each successive emperor, though they maintained the status of figurehead of the empire, had their powers very much reduced. Since then, 300 years of almost continuous civil war ensues between the <a href="/wiki/Yokeda" title="Yokeda">Yokeda</a> warlords, warrior monks and brigands, all fighting each other for land and power.<sup id="cite_ref-RHaH_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RHaH-29">[29]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_393">1E 393</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Holy Brothers of <a href="/wiki/Marukh" title="Marukh">Marukh</a> lead by Abbott Cosmas to <a href="/wiki/Malada" title="Malada">Malada</a>, with the intent of cleansing it.<sup id="cite_ref-Cleansing_26-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cleansing-26">[26]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDBR_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDBR-31">[31]</a></sup>
</li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_472">1E 472</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Kingdoms of <a href="/wiki/Skingrad" title="Skingrad">Skingrad</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kvatch" title="Kvatch">Kvatch</a> had formerly been at war with one another, but peace is declared in this year.<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li>It can be presumed that the children, Rislav and Belene, daughter of King Justinius of <a href="/wiki/Kvatch" title="Kvatch">Kvatch</a> were married here to make peace.<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_477">1E 477</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Clan_Direnni" title="Clan Direnni" class="mw-redirect">Clan Direnni</a> gains control of significant portions of Hammerfell and Skyrim.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_478">1E 478</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Sungard" title="Battle of Sungard">Battle of Sungard</a>: The High Chieftain of <a href="/wiki/Skyrim" title="Skyrim">Skyrim</a> (Kjoric the White) is killed by Emperor <a href="/wiki/Gorieus" title="Gorieus">Gorieus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Rislav_Larich" title="Rislav Larich">Rislav Larich</a> is known to be in <a href="/wiki/Kvatch" title="Kvatch">Kvatch</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Belene?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Belene (page does not exist)">Belene</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li>A great plague sweeps through <a href="/wiki/Cyrodiil" title="Cyrodiil">Cyrodiil</a>, wiping out King Mhorus and the rest of the Larich family, excepting Dorald, who had survived, as he was in <a href="/wiki/Imperial_City" title="Imperial City">Imperial City</a>, as a priest of <a href="/wiki/Marukh" title="Marukh">Marukh</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li>Dorald returns home and assumes the throne of King of <a href="/wiki/Skingrad" title="Skingrad">Skingrad</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li>Dorald cedes the kingdom of Skingrad to the Empire, as he had been taught by the <a href="/wiki/Alessia" title="Alessia">Alessian</a> monks of Marukh that "to resist the Empire was to resist the Gods."<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li>Rislav Larich rides from Kvatch with his wife and two dozen of the King of Kvatch's cavalry, which he defeats easily, as the guards hated the new ruler. He kills Dorald, and is crowned King of Kvatch.<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li>Rislav Larich vows to fight Emperor Gorieus, despite having little experience at either warfare or kingship. When Gorieus arrives, he tells him that his force is "too large for Skingrad" and to "Next time, write before you come."<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li>Rislav defeats the army of the Emperor, using archers to pick off an army that has no choice but to follow him.<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Direnni clan is inspired by these events and starts making plans to rebel.<sup id="cite_ref-Rislav_27-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rislav-27">[27]</a></sup>
</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="6th_Century">6th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_500">1E 500</span></h4>
<ul><li>A song is made about Wulfharth of Atmora. Following the death of King Hoag Merkiller of the Alessian armies at <a href="/wiki/Glenumbria_Moors" title="Glenumbria Moors" class="mw-redirect">Glenumbria Moors</a>, Wulfharth is made King following the Pact of Chieftains.<sup id="cite_ref-Shor.27s_Tongue_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Shor.27s_Tongue-35">[35]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-41">[40]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a> is freed from Aldmeri tyranny around this time.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:HR_0-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:HR-0">[1]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="7th_Century">7th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_609">1E 609</span></h4>
<ul><li>King Thagore of <a href="/wiki/Daggerfall" title="Daggerfall">Daggerfall</a> defeats the army of Glenpoint.<sup id="cite_ref-AHoD_1-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AHoD-1">[2]</a></sup>
</li><li>Daggerfall becomes "the preeminent economic, cultural, and military force in southern High Rock, a position the kingdom has precariously kept ever since."<sup id="cite_ref-AHoD_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AHoD-1">[2]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Mansel_Sesnit" title="Mansel Sesnit">Mansel Sesnit</a> becomes prominent in <a href="/wiki/Redguard" title="Redguard">Redguard</a> society.<sup id="cite_ref-RHaH_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RHaH-29">[29]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_617">1E 617</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Mansel_Sesnit" title="Mansel Sesnit">Mansel Sesnit</a> is assassinated, and a commoner takes over the government. <a href="/wiki/Randic_Torn" title="Randic Torn">Randic Torn</a> continues Sesnit's work, solidifying much of the Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-RHaH_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RHaH-29">[29]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_660">1E 660</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Mauloch" title="Mauloch">Mauloch</a> is defeated at the Battle of Dragon Wall at this time, and legend credits the eruption of <a href="/wiki/Red_Mountain" title="Red Mountain">Red Mountain</a> eight years later to his ensuing rage.<sup id="cite_ref-VoFitE_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VoFitE-42">[41]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:M_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:M-18">[19]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_668">1E 668</span></h4>
<ul><li>Historian <a href="/wiki/Borgusilus_Mailer?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Borgusilus Mailer (page does not exist)">Borgusilus Mailer</a> theorizes that it was in this year that the Dwemer enclaves were called together by one of their powerful philosopher-sorcerers, possibly "Kagrenak," to embark on a great journey, one of such sublime profundity that they abandoned all their cities and lands to join the quest to foreign climes as an entire culture.<sup id="cite_ref-ATofD_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ATofD-43">[42]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Red_Mountain" title="Red Mountain">Red Mountain</a> erupts, and <a href="/wiki/Sun%27s_Death" title="Sun's Death">Sun's Death</a> occurs.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:M_18-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:M-18">[19]</a></sup>
</li><li>It is supposed that the "<a href="/wiki/Sun%27s_Death" title="Sun's Death">Sun's Death</a>" event greatly affected the <a href="/wiki/Nirnroot" title="Nirnroot">Nirnroot</a> plant species.<sup id="cite_ref-nirnroot_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nirnroot-44">[43]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_675">1E 675</span></h4>
<ul><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/Poison_Song,_Book_I" title="Poison Song, Book I">Poison Song</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-TPS:I_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TPS:I-45">[44]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="8th_Century">8th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_700">1E 700</span></h4>
<ul><li>A <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Break" title="Dragon Break">Dragon Break</a> occurs; as such, no account of what transpires at <a href="/wiki/Red_Mountain" title="Red Mountain">Red Mountain</a> in this year is necessarily any more accurate than any other.<sup id="cite_ref-WWYWTDB_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWYWTDB-46">[45]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Red_Mountain" title="Battle of Red Mountain">Battle of Red Mountain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:M_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:M-19">[20]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:H_37-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:H-37">[37]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DI1_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DI1-47">[46]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/War_of_the_First_Council" title="War of the First Council">War of the First Council</a> ends: A religious conflict between the secular Dunmer Houses <a href="/wiki/Dwemer" title="Dwemer">Dwemer</a> and <a href="/wiki/House_Dagoth" title="House Dagoth">Dagoth</a> and the orthodox Dunmer Houses <a href="/wiki/House_Indoril" title="House Indoril">Indoril</a>, <a href="/wiki/House_Redoran" title="House Redoran">Redoran</a>, <a href="/wiki/House_Dres" title="House Dres">Dres</a>, <a href="/wiki/House_Hlaalu" title="House Hlaalu">Hlaalu</a>, and <a href="/wiki/House_Telvanni" title="House Telvanni">Telvanni</a>. The First Council was the first pan-Dunmer governing body, which collapsed over disputes about sorceries and enchantments practiced by the Dwemer and declared profane by the other Houses."<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[47]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:M_19-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:M-19">[20]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:H_36-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:H-36">[36]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-41">[40]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[48]</a></sup>
</li><li>Disappearance of the Dwemer. ca. 1E700.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:H_36-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:H-36">[36]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DI1_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DI1-47">[46]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_720">1E 720</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Frandar_Hunding" title="Frandar Hunding">Frandar Hunding</a> (<a href="/wiki/Redguard" title="Redguard">Redguard</a>) was born in this approximate year.<sup id="cite_ref-RHaH_29-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RHaH-29">[29]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_734">1E 734</span></h4>
<ul><li>Frandar's father dies.<sup id="cite_ref-RHaH_29-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RHaH-29">[29]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_737">1E 737</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Randic_Torn" title="Randic Torn">Randic Torn</a> dies.<sup id="cite_ref-RHaH_29-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RHaH-29">[29]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_750">1E 750</span></h4>
<ul><li>By this approximate year, Frandar Hunding has won over ninety battles; having killed his opponents in each, he is deemed "virtually invincible with a sword."<sup id="cite_ref-RHaH_29-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RHaH-29">[29]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_760">1E 760</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Divad_The_Singer" title="Divad The Singer" class="mw-redirect">Divad The Singer</a>, Son of <a href="/wiki/Frandar_Hunding" title="Frandar Hunding">Frandar Hunding</a>, and "most well known of <a href="/wiki/Redguard" title="Redguard">Redguard</a> heroes," was born in this year.<sup id="cite_ref-Divad_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Divad-50">[49]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_771">1E 771</span></h4>
<ul><li>Divad the Singer enters the "Hall of the Virtues of War" and begins his training there.<sup id="cite_ref-Divad_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Divad-50">[49]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_776">1E 776</span></h4>
<ul><li>Divad the Singer leaves the "Hall of the Virtues of War" in anger, breaks his swords, and vows to "become an acrobat in a travelling circus."<sup id="cite_ref-Divad_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Divad-50">[49]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_780">1E 780</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Frandar_Hunding" title="Frandar Hunding">Frandar Hunding</a>, retired and living as a hermit in <a href="/wiki/Mount_Hattu" title="Mount Hattu" class="mw-redirect">Mount Hattu</a>, writes his book, the <i><a href="/wiki/Book_of_Circles" title="Book of Circles">Book of Circles</a></i>, a book for <a href="/wiki/Sword-Singers" title="Sword-Singers">Sword-Singers</a> to emulate his fighting style.<sup id="cite_ref-RHaH_29-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RHaH-29">[29]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_792">1E 792</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Hiradirge" title="Hiradirge">Hiradirge</a>, a rebel <a href="/wiki/Ansei" title="Ansei">Ansei</a> group, destroy <a href="/wiki/Yokuda" title="Yokuda">Yokuda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Y_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Y-51">[50]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="9th_Century">9th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_800">1E 800</span></h4>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_874">1E 874</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Thulgeg" title="Thulgeg">Thulgeg</a>'s army of Orcs and Goblins is forced to flee northeast after being stopped at <a href="/wiki/Bangkorai_Pass" title="Bangkorai Pass">Bangkorai Pass</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BSoHR_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BSoHR-56">[55]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="10th_Century">10th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_907">1E 907</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Peregrine_Direnni" title="Peregrine Direnni" class="mw-redirect">Peregrine Direnni</a> repels the Redguard invasion of <a href="/wiki/Balfiera" title="Balfiera" class="mw-redirect">Balfiera</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[56]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[57]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_947">1E 947</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Gaiden_Shinji" title="Gaiden Shinji">Gaiden Shinji</a> (Blademaster) is quoted as saying "The best techniques are passed on by the survivors."<sup id="cite_ref-TES:A_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:A-59">[58]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_948">1E 948</span></h4>
<ul><li>First official historical reference to <a href="/wiki/Wayrest" title="Wayrest">Wayrest</a>, a letter by King <a href="/wiki/Joile" title="Joile">Joile</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Gaiden_Shinji" title="Gaiden Shinji">Gaiden Shinji</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Diagna" title="Order of Diagna">Order of Diagna</a>, which reads: <i>"The Orcs have been much plaguing the Wayresters and impeding traffic to the heart of that land."</i><sup id="cite_ref-WJoB_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WJoB-52">[51]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_950">1E 950</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Siege_of_Orsinium" title="Siege of Orsinium">Siege of Orsinium</a> begins.<sup id="cite_ref-TPS:I_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TPS:I-45">[44]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PigChildren_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PigChildren-60">[59]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Newgate_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Newgate-61">[60]</a></sup> (This last reference mentions this occurrence, although, it does not make a reference of the year this occurred, and elsewhere, it suggests the events of the book took place in <a href="#1E_675">1E 675</a>)<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:H_37-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:H-37">[37]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:H_36-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:H-36">[36]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:HR_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:HR-54">[53]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:WR_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:WR-62">[61]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Gaiden_Shinji" title="Gaiden Shinji">Gaiden Shinji</a> and <a href="/wiki/Baloth_Bloodtusk" title="Baloth Bloodtusk">Baloth Bloodtusk</a> die a number of years later during the Siege of Orsinium, at the command of King Joile.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:O_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:O-63">[62]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_973">1E 973</span></h4>
<ul><li>The memory stone of <a href="/wiki/Makela_Leki" title="Makela Leki">Makela Leki</a> is found at Bankorai Pass in this year, which depicted the <a href="/wiki/Battle_at_Bankorai_Pass" title="Battle at Bankorai Pass" class="mw-redirect">Battle at Bankorai Pass</a> and the death of King Joile.<sup id="cite_ref-Makela_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Makela-64">[63]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_980">1E 980</span></h4>
<ul><li>The combined armies of <a href="/wiki/Daggerfall" title="Daggerfall">Daggerfall</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sentinel" title="Sentinel">Sentinel</a>, and the Order of Diagna combine, causing the fall of <a href="/wiki/Orsinium" title="Orsinium">Orsinium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-AHoD_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AHoD-1">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:O_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:O-63">[62]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:H_36-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:H-36">[36]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-VoFitE_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VoFitE-42">[41]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-WJoB_52-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WJoB-52">[51]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:HR_54-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:HR-54">[53]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PigChildren_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PigChildren-60">[59]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Newgate_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Newgate-61">[60]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:WR_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:WR-62">[61]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:O_63-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:O-63">[62]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Makela_64-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Makela-64">[63]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[64]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_983">1E 983</span></h4>
<ul><li>The city of <a href="/wiki/Evermore" title="Evermore">Evermore</a> is founded by the <a href="/wiki/River_Horse_Bretons?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="River Horse Bretons (page does not exist)">River Horse Bretons</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TRHoKE_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TRHoKE-66">[65]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Bjoulsae_River" title="Bjoulsae River">Bjoulsae River</a> opens and much trade occurs, spurring on technological advancements such as writing.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_989">1E 989</span></h4>
<ul><li>Wayrest has a significant boost in population and size, growing from a small village to a large city.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="11th_Century">11th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_1030">1E 1030</span></h4>
<ul><li>The legendary Reachman known as <a href="/wiki/Red_Eagle" title="Red Eagle">Red Eagle</a> is said to have existed around this time.<sup id="cite_ref-eagle_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eagle-67">[66]</a></sup>
</li><li>Empress <a href="/wiki/Hestra" title="Hestra">Hestra</a> attempts to expand the empire into <a href="/wiki/The_Reach" title="The Reach">The Reach</a> and <a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-eagle_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eagle-67">[66]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_1033">1E 1033</span></h4>
<ul><li>Empress <a href="/wiki/Hestra" title="Hestra">Hestra</a> demands "the head of the most infamous of the brigadiers," Red <a href="/wiki/Bramman" title="Bramman">Bramman</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:BM_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:BM-24">[25]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="12th_Century">12th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_1100">1E 1100</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Farangel_Gardner" title="Farangel Gardner" class="mw-redirect">Farangel Gardner</a>, from a successful mercantile family, is proclaimed as the first King of <a href="/wiki/Wayrest" title="Wayrest">Wayrest</a> after being accepted by ambassadors from the Camorian Empire. <i>The city would then have four major dynasties in later times: that of Gardner, Cumberland, Horley, and finally Septim.</i><sup id="cite_ref-WJoB_52-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WJoB-52">[51]</a></sup>
</li><li>Wayrest becomes a city-state.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_1102">1E 1102</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ceyran" title="Ceyran">Ceyran</a>, a minor <a href="/wiki/Ayleid" title="Ayleid">Ayleid</a> warlord, is killed by an unknown assassin.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[67]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_1188">1E 1188</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Fervidius_Tharn" title="Fervidius Tharn">Fervidius Tharn</a> becomes the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Marukhati_Selective" title="Marukhati Selective">Marukhati Selective</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HTON_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HTON-12">[13]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="13th_Century">13th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_1200">1E 1200</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Middle Dawn begins.<sup id="cite_ref-WWYWTDB2_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWYWTDB2-69">[OOG 2]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Marukhati_Selective" title="Marukhati Selective">Marukhati Selective</a> accidentally (or purposefully) create a <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Break" title="Dragon Break">Dragon Break</a> that lasts one thousand and eight years. The few texts that survive this period are known to conflict with each other greatly due to the lack of a linear timeline.<sup id="cite_ref-WWYWTDB_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWYWTDB-46">[45]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-WWYWTDB2_69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWYWTDB2-69">[OOG 2]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_1250">1E 1250</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <i><a href="/wiki/Encyclopedia_Tamrielica" title="Encyclopedia Tamrielica">Encyclopedia Tamrielica</a></i> suggests the end of the <a href="/wiki/Alessian_Order" title="Alessian Order">Alessian Order</a> occurs in this year.<sup id="cite_ref-TDBR_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDBR-31">[31]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="14th_Century">14th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_1301">1E 1301</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Sack_of_Skywatch" title="Sack of Skywatch">Sack of Skywatch</a> occurs, from the <a href="/wiki/Sloads" title="Sloads" class="mw-redirect">Sloads</a> of <a href="/wiki/Thras" title="Thras">Thras</a> attack on the <a href="/wiki/Summerset_Isles" title="Summerset Isles">Summerset Isles</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:SI_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:SI-70">[68]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="15th_Century">15th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_1427">1E 1427</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Duncreigh_Bridge" title="Battle of Duncreigh Bridge">Battle of Duncreigh Bridge</a>: The "famous victory" of <a href="/wiki/Anticlere" title="Anticlere">Anticlere</a>'s Duke over the neighboring hamlet of <a href="/wiki/Sensford" title="Sensford">Sensford</a> is celebrated in <a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a> each year by the people marching down Sensford's main street. This results in numerous injuries on both sides, even when it doesn't provoke a brief war between the two "knightly orders" of the two villages. The battle itself achieved nothing, because both villages still boast about their ruling families' antique lineage.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:HR_0-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:HR-0">[1]</a></sup>
</li></ul>

</li><li>Most of the historic texts of this time were destroyed during the War of Righteousness.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceB_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceB-53">[52]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TSoP:VII_71-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TSoP:VII-71">[69]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2702">1E 2702</span></h4>
<ul><li>Most of <a href="/wiki/Wayrest" title="Wayrest">Wayrest</a> is forced to move within the high walls of the city, to protect themselves against Pirates, the <a href="/wiki/Akaviri" title="Akaviri">Akaviri</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Thrassian_Plague" title="Thrassian Plague">Thrassian Plague</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WJoB_52-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WJoB-52">[51]</a></sup>

</li><li><a href="/wiki/Reman_Cyrodiil" title="Reman Cyrodiil">Reman Cyrodiil</a> becomes Emperor of the Cyrodilic Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:C_8-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:C-8">[9]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:M_19-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:M-19">[20]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Akavir_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Akavir-75">[73]</a></sup>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/The_Reach" title="The Reach">The Reach</a> is split between High Rock and Skyrim by Reman Cyrodiil in order to stop the Reachmen from forming plots against him, and to stop any one entity or group from gaining full control over the region's silver mines.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[OOG 3]</a></sup>
</li><li>Reman Cyrodiil solidifies his control over his territories.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:C_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:C-20">[21]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2705">1E 2705</span></h4>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2720">1E 2720</span></h4>
<ul><li>A commander of the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Legion" title="Imperial Legion">Imperial Legion</a> stationed in <a href="/wiki/Reman%27s_Bluff" title="Reman's Bluff">Reman's Bluff</a>, Valenwood, has his forces reduced to 20 men. He abstains from sending out hunting parties due to the <a href="/wiki/Wood_Orcs" title="Wood Orcs">Wood Orcs</a> that pose a threat.<sup id="cite_ref-TFaRoRB_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TFaRoRB-78">[75]</a></sup>
</li><li>One of his soldiers later shoots an Orsimer Shaman, who was travelling to Reman's Bluff with the intention of brokering a peace agreement.<sup id="cite_ref-TFaRoRB_78-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TFaRoRB-78">[75]</a></sup>
</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="29th_Century">29th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2801">1E 2801</span></h4>
<ul><li>Kastav rules the Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li><li>Kastav orders the seizing of hostages in <a href="/wiki/Markarth" title="Markarth">Markarth</a> and <a href="/wiki/Old_Hroldan" title="Old Hroldan" class="mw-redirect">Hroldan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2804">1E 2804</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Winterhold_Rebellion" title="Winterhold Rebellion">Winterhold Rebellion</a> breaks out in the <a href="/wiki/Reman_Empire" title="Reman Empire">Reman Empire</a> due to the implementation of extremely high taxes by Emperor <a href="/wiki/Kastav" title="Kastav">Kastav</a>, and harsh policies to ensure that said taxes were paid. The Dragonguard take no action,—because doing so would violate their Oath of Allegiance—so supplies to them are cut.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Reachmen" title="Reachmen">Reachmen</a> are noted as helping the <a href="/wiki/Akaviri" title="Akaviri">Akaviri</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sky_Haven_Temple" title="Sky Haven Temple">Sky Haven Temple</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2805">1E 2805</span></h4>
<ul><li>Emperor Kastav besieges Sky Haven Temple.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Kalien" title="Kalien">Kalien</a>, a failed recruit to the Dragonguard, attacks <a href="/wiki/Winterhold" title="Winterhold">Winterhold</a>, sacking it.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2806">1E 2806</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Reman_Cyrodiil_II" title="Reman Cyrodiil II">Reman Cyrodiil II</a> becomes Emperor, according to the <i><a href="/wiki/Annals_of_the_Dragonguard" title="Annals of the Dragonguard">Annals of the Dragonguard</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li><li>The siege on <a href="/wiki/Sky_Haven_Temple" title="Sky Haven Temple">Sky Haven Temple</a> is lifted.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2809">1E 2809</span></h4>
<ul><li>Reports of a <a href="/wiki/Dragons_(Lore)" title="Dragons (Lore)">Dragon</a> in <a href="/wiki/Skyrim" title="Skyrim">Skyrim</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2811">1E 2811</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Argonia" title="Battle of Argonia">Battle of Argonia</a> is fought, and the Cyrodilic Empire defeats the Argonians in what is to be their last organized army.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:BM_24-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:BM-24">[25]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Argonian" title="Argonian">Argonians</a> retreat to <a href="/wiki/Helstrom" title="Helstrom">Helstrom</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:BM_24-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:BM-24">[25]</a></sup>
</li><li>General Bucco takes command of the Fourth Imperial Legion and begins his campaign to conquer the inner swamps of Argonia.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW1_84-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW1-84">[79]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2812">1E 2812</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Reman_Cyrodiil_II" title="Reman Cyrodiil II">Reman Cyrodiil II</a> is crowned Emperor, according to his tomb in <a href="/wiki/Sancre_Tor" title="Sancre Tor">Sancre Tor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-RCIITomb_82-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RCIITomb-82">[78]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Black_Marsh" title="Black Marsh">Black Marsh</a> is officially incorporated into the Cyrodilic Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:BM_24-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:BM-24">[25]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Alduin%27s_Wall_(Lore)" title="Alduin's Wall (Lore)">Alduin's Wall</a> officially begins construction.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2813">1E 2813</span></h4>
<ul><li>Work on Alduin's wall slows when several craftsmen are dismissed from service.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li><li>The language Cyrodilic replaces High Elven as the dominant language for legal documents in Tamriel.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2815">1E 2815</span></h4>
<ul><li>Grandmaster of the Dragonguard visits <a href="/wiki/Sky_Haven_Temple" title="Sky Haven Temple">Sky Haven Temple</a>, to investigate rumors of the cost of Alduin's Wall, and consequently writes a Writ of Requisition for more supplies.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2816">1E 2816</span></h4>
<ul><li>General Bucco's legion is depleted to a mere six cohorts. Reinforcements are brought in to aid his conquest but are instead used to build a supply highway.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW3_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW3-85">[80]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2818">1E 2818</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Alduin%27s_Wall_(Lore)" title="Alduin's Wall (Lore)">Alduin's Wall</a> officially completed.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2820">1E 2820</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Eric_of_Guis" title="Eric of Guis">Eric of Guis</a> is Ambassador of the <a href="/wiki/Reman_Dynasty" title="Reman Dynasty">Reman Dynasty</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Altmer" title="Altmer">Altmer</a> of <a href="/wiki/Summerset_Isles" title="Summerset Isles">Summerset Isles</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:AD_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:AD-28">[28]</a></sup>
</li><li>After an attempted mutiny, General Bucco orders a retreat from Argonia. The entire <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Legion" title="Fourth Legion">Fourth Legion</a> is lost in the process, with Bucco along with it.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW4_86-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW4-86">[81]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Elder Council reconstitutes the Fourth Legion and puts it under the command of General Regulus Sardecus, beginning the second campaign of the <a href="/wiki/Blackwater_War" title="Blackwater War">Blackwater War</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW4_86-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW4-86">[81]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2823">1E 2823</span></h4>
<ul><li>General Sardecus reacquires all the territory lost in General Bucco's retreat.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW5_87-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW5-87">[82]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2828">1E 2828</span></h4>
<ul><li>A widespread forest fire, later known as the "Great Burn" occurs in Black Marsh, forcing General Sardecus to retreat from the region. Sardecus dies in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW6_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW6-88">[83]</a></sup>
</li><li>General Lucinia Falco is placed in command of the legion shortly after Sardecus' death.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW7_89-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW7-89">[84]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2833">1E 2833</span></h4>
<ul><li>The "Falco Doctrine" is put in full effect, completely revising the Imperial battle-plan in the Blackwater War.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW7_89-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW7-89">[84]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2834">1E 2834</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Blackwater War evolves into a guerilla conflict.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW7_89-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW7-89">[84]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2836">1E 2836</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Argonians inexplicably stop fighting and return to their homes, bringing an informal end to the Blackwater war.<sup id="cite_ref-TBWW7_89-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW7-89">[84]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2837">1E 2837</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Second Empire annexation of Argonia is complete, officially creating the province of <a href="/wiki/Black_Marsh" title="Black Marsh">Black Marsh</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:WR_62-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:WR-62">[61]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TBWW7_89-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBWW7-89">[84]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2840">1E 2840</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Four_Score_War" title="Four Score War">Four Score War</a> begins, between <a href="/wiki/Morrowind" title="Morrowind">Morrowind</a> and the Cyrodilic Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:M_19-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:M-19">[20]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1E_2843">1E 2843</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Reman_Cyrodiil_II" title="Reman Cyrodiil II">Reman Cyrodiil II</a> dies, according to <i><a href="/wiki/Reman_II:_The_Limits_of_Ambition" title="Reman II: The Limits of Ambition">Reman II: The Limits of Ambition</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-RII:LA_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RII:LA-90">[85]</a></sup>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_230">2E 230</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Mages_Guild" title="Mages Guild">Mages Guild</a> is formed by <a href="/wiki/Vanus_Galerion" title="Vanus Galerion">Vanus Galerion</a> (formerly known as "Trechtus").<sup id="cite_ref-MGC_101-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MGC-101">[95]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[96]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[97]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">[98]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">[99]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">[100]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_283">2E 283</span></h4>
<ul><li>Potentate <a href="/wiki/Versidue_Shaie" title="Versidue Shaie">Versidue Shaie</a>, ruler of Tamriel, is faced with a disintegrating empire, with "the vassal kingdoms throughout Tamriel reaching a new height of rebellion and openly challenging his rule."<sup id="cite_ref-HistFG_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HistFG-72">[70]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FGH_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FGH-73">[71]</a></sup>
</li><li>The kingdoms refuse to pay taxes, and lead sorties against Imperial garrisons in many countries.<sup id="cite_ref-HistFG_72-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HistFG-72">[70]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FGH_73-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FGH-73">[71]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Imperial fortress <a href="/wiki/Dawnstar" title="Dawnstar">Dawnstar</a> is destroyed.<sup id="cite_ref-HistFG_72-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HistFG-72">[70]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FGH_73-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FGH-73">[71]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Council_of_Bardmont" title="Council of Bardmont">Council of Bardmont</a> is held, whereby the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Council?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Imperial Council (page does not exist)">Imperial Council</a> is gathered, and martial law is declared.<sup id="cite_ref-FGH_73-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FGH-73">[71]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_283_-_2E_320">2E 283 - 2E 320</span></h4>
<ul><li>Potentate Versidue-Shaie begins a bloody process of wiping away all opposing resistance to the Empire, expending the majority of his legions, and nearly all of the Imperial gold, in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-HistFG_72-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HistFG-72">[70]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FGH_73-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FGH-73">[71]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="4th_Century_2">4th Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_309">2E 309</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Elsweyr" title="Elsweyr">Elsweyr</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Khajiit" title="Khajiit">Khajiit</a> kingdom, is created after Keirgo of Anequina and Eshita of Pellitine combined their long-feuding kingdoms, and created a class struggle that briefly threatened to draw in outside intervention.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:E_23-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:E-23">[24]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:EC_107-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:EC-107">[101]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_320">2E 320</span></h4>
<ul><li>Dinieras-Ves "The Iron," a relation of <a href="/wiki/Versidue_Shaie" title="Versidue Shaie">Versidue Shaie</a>, presented both himself and a host of warriors before the Potentate, suggesting an order of mercantile warriors-for-hire, who could be hired by nobility in lieu of a standing army, and that the "employment would be temporary, and a percentage of the fee would go to the Potentate's government, thus putting salve on two of Versidae-Shaie's (sic) greatest pains.<sup id="cite_ref-HistFG_72-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HistFG-72">[70]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FGH_73-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FGH-73">[71]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_321">2E 321</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Guilds_Act" title="Guilds Act">Guilds Act</a> is passed: <i>"In the 321st year of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Era" title="Second Era">Second Era</a>, the Potentate gave his approval to the <a href="/wiki/Guilds_Act" title="Guilds Act">Guilds Act</a>, officially sanctioning the <a href="/wiki/Mages_Guild" title="Mages Guild">Mages</a>, together with the Guilds of Tinkers, Cobblers, Prostitutes, Scribes, Architects, Brewers, Vintners, Weavers, Ratcatchers, Furriers, Cooks, Astrologers, Healers, Tailors, Minstrals (sic), Barristers, and the Syffim."</i><sup id="cite_ref-HistFG_72-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HistFG-72">[70]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FGH_73-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FGH-73">[71]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Fighters_Guild" title="Fighters Guild">The Guild of Fighters</a> was established under the section four of the "Guilds Act," the charter first confirmed under <a href="/wiki/Potentate" title="Potentate">Potentate</a> <a href="/wiki/Versidue_Shaie" title="Versidue Shaie">Versidue-Shaie</a> in this year.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">[102]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_324">2E 324</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Morag_Tong" title="Morag Tong">Morag Tong</a> assassinate Potentate <a href="/wiki/Versidue_Shaie" title="Versidue Shaie">Versidue Shaie</a>. The Morag Tong had become so drunk with murder that they literally wrote the words "Morag Tong" in blood on the walls.<sup id="cite_ref-FaD:TBoD_95-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FaD:TBoD-95">[89]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TBoD_109-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBoD-109">[103]</a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li><li>Morag Tong is outlawed throughout Tamriel.<sup id="cite_ref-FaD:TBoD_95-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FaD:TBoD-95">[89]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li><li>Shortly after the eradication of the <a href="/wiki/Morag_Tong" title="Morag Tong">Morag Tong</a> in Cyrodiil, a Dunmer woman serving the faction, who later became the <a href="/wiki/Night_Mother" title="Night Mother">Night Mother</a>, hears the voice of <a href="/wiki/Sithis_(Deity)" title="Sithis (Deity)">Sithis</a>. Sithis then later visited the Night Mother and begat to her five children.<sup id="cite_ref-TNMT_110-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TNMT-110">[104]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_326">2E 326</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Night Mother kills her young children, and send their souls to the <a href="/wiki/Void" title="Void">Void</a>, back to their father Sithis. She is later murdered by the people of the village for her horrid act.<sup id="cite_ref-TNMT_110-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TNMT-110">[104]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_342">2E 342</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/King_Donel_Deleyn" title="King Donel Deleyn">Donel Deleyn</a> is crowned king of <a href="/wiki/Daggerfall" title="Daggerfall">Daggerfall</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TIEGT_HighRock_111-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TIEGT_HighRock-111">[105]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_358">2E 358</span></h4>
<ul><li>A note about the <a href="/wiki/Morag_Tong" title="Morag Tong">Morag Tong</a> is found beneath the floorboards of an abandoned house in the <a href="/wiki/Nord" title="Nord">Nordic</a> village of <a href="/wiki/Jallenheim" title="Jallenheim">Jallenheim</a> in this year. It was said that the house had belonged to "a quiet cobbler, who was whispered by some to have been a Morag Tong member."<sup id="cite_ref-FaD:TBoD_95-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FaD:TBoD-95">[89]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_406">2E 406</span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_409">2E 409</span></h4>

After recovering, he holds a funeral for the deceased servant. <a href="/wiki/Magiul_Shiana?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Magiul Shiana (page does not exist)">Magiul Shiana</a>, the royal cook, is chosen as the next Seneschal.<sup id="cite_ref-JoMS_114-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JoMS-114">[108]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_412">2E 412</span></h4>

However, it is possible that the organization existed before 2E 360.<sup id="cite_ref-TBoD_109-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBoD-109">[103]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_420">2E 420</span></h4>

</li></ul>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_430">2E 430</span></h4>
<ul><li>The period known as the <a href="/wiki/Interregnum" title="Interregnum">Interregnum</a> begins.<sup id="cite_ref-TBoD_109-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBoD-109">[103]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Akaviri_Potentate" title="Akaviri Potentate" class="mw-redirect">Akaviri Potentate</a> <a href="/wiki/Savirien_Chorak" title="Savirien Chorak">Savirien Chorak</a> dies.<sup id="cite_ref-TBoD_109-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TBoD-109">[103]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_431">2E 431</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Second_Sacking_of_Orsinium?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Second Sacking of Orsinium (page does not exist)">Second Sacking of Orsinium</a> occurs.<sup id="cite_ref-TRHoKE_66-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TRHoKE-66">[65]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Reman_Empire" title="Reman Empire">Reman Empire</a> is been completely dissolved due to civil wars and insurrections.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_434">2E 434</span></h4>
<ul><li>King <a href="/wiki/Maxevian?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Maxevian (page does not exist)">Maxevian</a> forms the <a href="/wiki/Pale_Watch" title="Pale Watch">Pale Watch</a>, and tasks them with guarding <a href="/wiki/Watcher%27s_Hold" title="Watcher's Hold">Watcher's Hold</a> for an intended five years, in order to make sure the Orcs do not return to <a href="/wiki/Wrothgar" title="Wrothgar">Wrothgar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-KMO_116-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KMO-116">[110]</a></sup>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_442">2E 442</span></h4>
<ul><li>Months after a communique, the Pale Watch begin to grow restless, with some crowing about abandoning Watcher's Hold. The Watchmaster orders the scourging of two soldiers for seditious talk.<sup id="cite_ref-RWJ_118-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RWJ-118">[112]</a></sup>

The second Daggerfall Covenant was signed in <a href="#2E_567">2E 567</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GDC_126-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GDC-126">[119]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_560">2E 560</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Knahaten_Flu" title="Knahaten Flu">Knahaten Flu</a> begins, initiated at <a href="/wiki/Stormhold" title="Stormhold">Stormhold</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:WR_62-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:WR-62">[61]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE1:EC_107-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1:EC-107">[101]</a></sup>
</li><li>Knahaten Flu spreads quickly to the rest of <a href="/wiki/Black_Marsh" title="Black Marsh">Black Marsh</a>, harshly affecting the population there. Strangely, the Argonians were immune to the flu.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:BM_24-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:BM-24">[25]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_561">2E 561</span></h4>
