</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_563">2E 563</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Altmer" title="Altmer">Altmer</a> <a href="/wiki/Princess_Ayrenn" title="Princess Ayrenn" class="mw-redirect">Princess Ayrenn</a> disappears on the way to the <a href="/wiki/College_of_Aldmeri_Propriety" title="College of Aldmeri Propriety">College of Aldmeri Propriety</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Ayrenn_128-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ayrenn-128">[121]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Crimson_Ship" title="Crimson Ship">Crimson Ship</a> flees <a href="/wiki/Black_Marsh" title="Black Marsh">Black Marsh</a>, loaded with flu-infected <a href="/wiki/Kothringi" title="Kothringi">Kothringi</a> refugees. After being turned away from every port, they were never seen again,<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup> barring an encounter with a few pirates who found only a dead crew.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">[124]</a></sup> This tragedy is remembered by the <a href="/wiki/Day_of_Shame" title="Day of Shame">Day of Shame</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hammerfell" title="Hammerfell">Hammerfell</a>, where no one leaves their houses.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">[125]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Emeric" title="Emeric" class="mw-redirect">Emeric</a> is crowned King of <a href="/wiki/Wayrest" title="Wayrest">Wayrest</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Ranser_War_133-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ranser_War-133">[126]</a></sup>
</li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_567">2E 567</span></h4>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_568">2E 568</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <i><a href="/wiki/Annals_of_the_Dragonguard" title="Annals of the Dragonguard">Annals of the Dragonguard</a></i> are written.<sup id="cite_ref-AofD_77-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AofD-77">[74]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_572">2E 572</span></h4>
<ul><li>A massive force of <a href="/wiki/Akaviri" title="Akaviri">Akaviri</a> led by <a href="/wiki/Ada%27Soom_Dir-Kamal" title="Ada'Soom Dir-Kamal">Ada'Soom Dir-Kamal</a> lands in <a href="/wiki/Skyrim" title="Skyrim">Skyrim</a> and immediately sacks the city of <a href="/wiki/Windhelm" title="Windhelm">Windhelm</a>, causing the death of <a href="/wiki/Nurnhilde" title="Nurnhilde">Nurnhilde</a>, sister of <a href="/wiki/Jorunn" title="Jorunn" class="mw-redirect">Jorunn</a>, and Jorunn's mother <a href="/wiki/Mabjaarn" title="Mabjaarn" class="mw-redirect">Mabjaarn</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">[128]</a></sup>
</li><li>A large army led by Jorunn and <a href="/wiki/Wulfharth_the_Ash-King" title="Wulfharth the Ash-King" class="mw-redirect">Wulfharth the Ash-King</a>, march to <a href="/wiki/Riften_(Online)" title="Riften (Online)">Riften</a>. After Dir-Kamal learned that Riften was fortified, he bypassed the city and attacked <a href="/wiki/Mournhold_(Online)" title="Mournhold (Online)">Mournhold</a> instead.<sup id="cite_ref-JorunnBook_127-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JorunnBook-127">[120]</a></sup>
</li><li>Dir-Kamal was then trapped between Jorunn and Wulfharth's forces and a <a href="/wiki/Dunmer" title="Dunmer">Dunmeri</a> army led by <a href="/wiki/Almalexia_(God)" title="Almalexia (God)" class="mw-redirect">Almalexia</a>. With the timely aid of a phalanx of <a href="/wiki/Argonian" title="Argonian">Argonian</a> battlemages, the Akaviri were driven into the sea where they drowned by the thousands.<sup id="cite_ref-JorunnBook_127-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JorunnBook-127">[120]</a></sup>
</li><li>Jorunn is crowned <a href="/wiki/High_King" title="High King">High King</a> of Skyrim.<sup id="cite_ref-JorunnBook_127-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JorunnBook-127">[120]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Ebonheart_Pact" title="Ebonheart Pact">Ebonheart Pact</a> is formed during the fight against the <a href="/wiki/Akaviri" title="Akaviri">Akaviri</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">[129]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">[130]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_573">2E 573</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Varen_Aquilarios" title="Varen Aquilarios">Varen Aquilarios</a> overthrows Emperor Leovic, last of the dynasty of <a href="/wiki/Reachmen" title="Reachmen">Reachmen</a> known as the Longhouse Emperors, and conquers <a href="/wiki/Cyrodiil" title="Cyrodiil">Cyrodiil</a>. After legalizing <a href="/wiki/Daedra" title="Daedra">Daedra</a> worship, Varen sparked a rebellion against Leovic. After a long and bloody war, Varen kills Leovic in his throne room and declares himself <a href="/wiki/Emperor" title="Emperor">Emperor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">[131]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_576">2E 576</span></h4>
<ul><li>Varen Aquilarios seeks to legitimize his claim to the <a href="/wiki/Ruby_Throne" title="Ruby Throne">Ruby Throne</a> and forms the <a href="/wiki/Five_Companions" title="Five Companions">Five Companions</a> to find the long-lost <a href="/wiki/Amulet_of_Kings" title="Amulet of Kings">Amulet of Kings</a> in the hopes that Varen could make himself <a href="/wiki/Dragonborn_(Lore)" title="Dragonborn (Lore)">Dragonborn</a>. The Five Companions consisted of <a href="/wiki/Lyris_Titanborn" title="Lyris Titanborn">Lyris Titanborn</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mannimarco_(Online)" title="Mannimarco (Online)">Mannimarco</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sai_Sahan" title="Sai Sahan">Sai Sahan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Varen_Aquilarios" title="Varen Aquilarios">Varen Aquilarios</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Abnur_Tharn" title="Abnur Tharn">Abnur Tharn</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">[132]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_578">2E 578</span></h4>
<ul><li>After two years of searching, the <a href="/wiki/Five_Companions" title="Five Companions">Five Companions</a> finally recover the <a href="/wiki/Amulet_of_Kings" title="Amulet of Kings">Amulet of Kings</a> from <a href="/wiki/Sancre_Tor" title="Sancre Tor">Sancre Tor</a>.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Wiki:Sourcing" title="The Elder Scrolls Wiki:Sourcing"><i>source?</i></a>&#93;</sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Soulburst" title="Soulburst">Soulburst</a> takes place. <a href="/wiki/Mannimarco_(Online)" title="Mannimarco (Online)">Mannimarco</a>, one of the Five Companions, betrays Varen Aquilarios during his attempt to use the <a href="/wiki/Amulet_of_Kings" title="Amulet of Kings">Amulet of Kings</a> to become Dragonborn, corrupting the ritual and breaking the covenant with <a href="/wiki/Akatosh" title="Akatosh">Akatosh</a> that sealed <a href="/wiki/Nirn" title="Nirn">Nirn</a> from <a href="/wiki/Oblivion_(Realm)" title="Oblivion (Realm)">Oblivion</a>. A massive explosion of arcane energy, the Soulburst, erupted in the Imperial City, causing Varen to vanish. Mystical aftershocks swept across Nirn, causing mages to die or go mad. The Daedra appeared in greater numbers than ever before and the constellation of the Serpent, signifying chaos, appeared so large that it dominated the night sky.<sup id="cite_ref-Facebook_140-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Facebook-140">[OOG 5]</a></sup>
</li><li>The barrier between Nirn and Oblivion is destroyed, allowing <a href="/wiki/Molag_Bal" title="Molag Bal">Molag Bal</a> to begin the <a href="/wiki/Planemeld" title="Planemeld">Planemeld</a> and begin deploying <a href="/wiki/Dark_Anchors" title="Dark Anchors">Dark Anchors</a> into Tamriel to merge Nirn and <a href="/wiki/Coldharbour" title="Coldharbour">Coldharbour</a> together into one single, nightmarish hellscape.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Wiki:Sourcing" title="The Elder Scrolls Wiki:Sourcing"><i>source?</i></a>&#93;</sup>
</li><li>The Five Companions flee and split up. Varen wakes up outside the <a href="/wiki/Cult_of_the_Ancestor_Moth" title="Cult of the Ancestor Moth">Abbey of the Moth Priests</a> with no memory of his identity, and begins studying the Elder Scrolls. Lyris is captured by Molag Bal, and she is sent to Coldharbour as a slave. Sai Sahan fled and managed to hide the Amulet of Kings in Sancre Tor, but later on he too suffered the same fate as Lyris. Mannimarco begun sacrificing souls to Molag Bal, including the <a href="/wiki/Vestige" title="Vestige">Vestige</a>'s. Abnur Tharn fled and continued to rule as Overlord of Nibenay.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Wiki:Sourcing" title="The Elder Scrolls Wiki:Sourcing"><i>source?</i></a>&#93;</sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Clivia_Tharn" title="Clivia Tharn">Clivia Tharn</a> assumes the role of Empress Regent in the absence of her husband Varen.<sup id="cite_ref-TM10_141-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TM10-141">[133]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_580">2E 580</span></h4>
<ul><li>Altmer King <a href="/wiki/Hidellith" title="Hidellith">Hidellith</a> dies.<sup id="cite_ref-Ayrenn_128-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ayrenn-128">[121]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Queen_Ayrenn" title="Queen Ayrenn">Queen Ayrenn</a> returns to <a href="/wiki/Summerset_Isles" title="Summerset Isles">Summerset Isles</a>, and becomes Queen of Alinor. After seeing the instability and chaos in Tamriel caused by man, she forms an alliance with <a href="/wiki/Valenwood" title="Valenwood">Valenwood</a> and <a href="/wiki/Elsweyr" title="Elsweyr">Elsweyr</a> to create the <a href="/wiki/Aldmeri_Dominion_(Online)" title="Aldmeri Dominion (Online)">Aldmeri Dominion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Ayrenn_128-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ayrenn-128">[121]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Three_Banners_War" title="Three Banners War" class="mw-redirect">Three Banners War</a> begins between the <a href="/wiki/First_Aldmeri_Dominion" title="First Aldmeri Dominion" class="mw-redirect">First Aldmeri Dominion</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Daggerfall_Covenant" title="Daggerfall Covenant">Daggerfall Covenant</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Ebonheart_Pact" title="Ebonheart Pact">Ebonheart Pact</a>, sparking one of the most brutal conflicts Tamriel has ever seen.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Wiki:Sourcing" title="The Elder Scrolls Wiki:Sourcing"><i>source?</i></a>&#93;</sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_581">2E 581</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Captain_Rana" title="Captain Rana">Captain Rana</a> is stationed at <a href="/wiki/Bleakrock_Isle" title="Bleakrock Isle">Bleakrock Isle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-RanaLog_142-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RanaLog-142">[134]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_582">2E 582</span></h4>
<ul><li>Events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Online" title="The Elder Scrolls Online">The Elder Scrolls Online</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-ESO_143-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESO-143">[135]</a></sup>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Molag_Bal" title="Molag Bal">Molag Bal</a> is defeated by the <a href="/wiki/Vestige" title="Vestige">Vestige</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Planemeld" title="Planemeld">Planemeld</a> ends.<sup id="cite_ref-ESO_143-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESO-143">[135]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Eyevea" title="Eyevea">Eyevea</a>, an island haven of the <a href="/wiki/Summerset_Isles" title="Summerset Isles">Summerset Isles</a> owned by <a href="/wiki/Arch-Mage_Shalidor" title="Arch-Mage Shalidor">Arch-Mage Shalidor</a> during the First Era, is returned by Sheogorath to Tamriel, thanks to the Vestige and <a href="/wiki/Valaste" title="Valaste">Valaste</a> of the Mages Guild.<sup id="cite_ref-ESO_143-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESO-143">[135]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Mortuum_Vivicus" title="Mortuum Vivicus">Mortuum Vivicus</a> is successfully destroyed by the Fighters Guild.<sup id="cite_ref-ESO_143-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESO-143">[135]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
</li><li>Events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Online:_Imperial_City" title="The Elder Scrolls Online: Imperial City">The Elder Scrolls Online: Imperial City</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-IC_144-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IC-144">[136]</a></sup>
<ul><li>Molag Bal's <a href="/wiki/Dark_anchor" title="Dark anchor" class="mw-redirect">Dark anchor</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_City" title="Imperial City">Imperial City</a> is destroyed by the Vestige and <a href="/wiki/Sister_Terran_Arminus" title="Sister Terran Arminus">Sister Terran Arminus</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Xivkyn" title="Xivkyn">Xivkyn</a> <a href="/wiki/Molag_Kena" title="Molag Kena">Molag Kena</a> masquerading as <a href="/wiki/Empress" title="Empress" class="mw-redirect">Empress</a> <a href="/wiki/Clivia_Tharn" title="Clivia Tharn">Clivia Tharn</a> is killed.<sup id="cite_ref-IC_144-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IC-144">[136]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Sublime_Brazier?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Sublime Brazier (page does not exist)">Sublime Brazier</a>, a contraption that powers the <a href="/wiki/Dragonfires" title="Dragonfires">Dragonfires</a>, is saved by the Vestige and the <a href="/wiki/Drake_of_Blades" title="Drake of Blades">Drake of Blades</a> from Molag Bal's plan to destroy it.<sup id="cite_ref-IC_144-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IC-144">[136]</a></sup>
</li><li>Molag Bal's grip on the Imperial City is successfully ended, saving it from the Planemeld.<sup id="cite_ref-IC_144-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IC-144">[136]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_583">2E 583</span></h4>
<ul><li>Events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Online:_Orsinium" title="The Elder Scrolls Online: Orsinium">The Elder Scrolls Online: Orsinium</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-OR_145-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OR-145">[137]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BoW_146-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BoW-146">[138]</a></sup>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/King_Kurog" title="King Kurog">King Kurog</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Orsinium" title="Second Orsinium" class="mw-redirect">Second Orsinium</a> and the Vestige kill <a href="/wiki/Urfon_Ice-Heart" title="Urfon Ice-Heart">Urfon Ice-Heart</a>, ending the <a href="/wiki/Winterborn" title="Winterborn" class="mw-redirect">Winterborn</a> threat against <a href="/wiki/Wrothgar" title="Wrothgar">Wrothgar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OR_145-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OR-145">[137]</a></sup>
</li><li>Invitations to a <a href="/wiki/Moot" title="Moot">Moot</a> held by King Kurog are accepted by <a href="/wiki/Orsimer" title="Orsimer">Orsimer</a> clan chiefs, <a href="/wiki/Chief_Bazrag" title="Chief Bazrag">Chief Bazrag</a> is saved from the <a href="/wiki/Vosh_Rakh_(Faction)" title="Vosh Rakh (Faction)">Vosh Rakh</a>, and the Vosh Rakh's infiltration of the Second Orsinium is unveiled.<sup id="cite_ref-OR_145-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OR-145">[137]</a></sup>
</li><li>King Kurog is killed after his betrayal is revealed, with his plot to kill the clan chiefs foiled, and <a href="/wiki/Bazrag_gro-Fharun" title="Bazrag gro-Fharun" class="mw-redirect">Bazrag gro-Fharun</a> is crowned the new king of the Second Orsinium.<sup id="cite_ref-OR_145-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OR-145">[137]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_852">2E 852</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Sancre_Tor" title="Battle of Sancre Tor">Battle of Sancre Tor</a> takes place, with <a href="/wiki/Nord" title="Nord">Nord</a> and <a href="/wiki/Breton" title="Breton">Breton</a> forces crossing the borders into <a href="/wiki/Cyrodiil" title="Cyrodiil">Cyrodiil</a>. They set up their headquarters at Sancre Tor, and taunt <a href="/wiki/Cuhlecain" title="Cuhlecain">Cuhlecain</a>'s general, <a href="/wiki/Tiber_Septim" title="Tiber Septim">Talos</a>, into attacking them.<sup id="cite_ref-LCST_17-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LCST-17">[18]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">[143]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_854">2E 854</span></h4>
<ul><li>Breton assassins decide to counterattack Talos, and set fire to the Imperial Palace, with Cuhlecain inside it; they also "slit the throat of General Talos." However, "from the smoldering ruin he came, one hand to his neck and with Cuhlecain's Crown in the other."<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1_34-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1-34">[34]</a></sup>
</li><li>One of two possible dates when Tiber Septim began his conquest of Tamriel.<sup id="cite_ref-BHoE:I_151-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BHoE:I-151">[142]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2E_855">2E 855</span></h4>
<ul><li>General Talos has already changed his name to <a href="/wiki/Tiber_Septim" title="Tiber Septim">Tiber Septim</a>. 
</li><li>Second possible date when Tiber Septim began <a href="/wiki/Tiber_Wars" title="Tiber Wars">his conquest of Tamriel</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-IaC_155-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IaC-155">[144]</a></sup>
</li><li>One of General Talos' commanders, Beatia of Ylliolos, and her Lieutenant, Ascutus, are ambushed on their way to Porhnak, where a Legion was stationed. They are ambushed by <a href="/wiki/Nord" title="Nord">Nords</a> ("the warchiefs of Danstra").<sup id="cite_ref-IaC_155-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IaC-155">[144]</a></sup>

</li><li><a href="/wiki/Hammerfell" title="Hammerfell">Hammerfell</a> joins the Septim Empire,<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:H_37-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:H-37">[37]</a></sup>, although concessions are later made after a revolt in <a href="/wiki/Stros_M%27kai" title="Stros M'kai">Stros M'kai</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:H_37-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:H-37">[37]</a></sup>
</li><li>The story of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Adventures:_Redguard" title="The Elder Scrolls Adventures: Redguard">The Elder Scrolls Adventures: Redguard</a></i> takes place.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:R_156-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:R-156">[145]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:F_157-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:F-157">[146]</a></sup>

</li><li><a href="/wiki/N%27Gasta" title="N'Gasta">N'Gasta</a>, a powerful <a href="/wiki/Sload" title="Sload">Sload</a> <a href="/wiki/Necromancer" title="Necromancer">necromancer</a>, is killed by Cyrus on <a href="/wiki/Stros_M%27Kai" title="Stros M'Kai" class="mw-redirect">Stros M'Kai</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">[148]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
</li><li>The <i><a href="/wiki/Pocket_Guide_to_the_Empire,_First_Edition" title="Pocket Guide to the Empire, First Edition">Pocket Guide to the Empire, First Edition</a></i> is published by the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Geographic_Society" title="Imperial Geographic Society">Imperial Geographic Society</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE1_34-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE1-34">[34]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_63">3E 63</span></h4>

Instead, he learns about a werewolf that is plaguing the city, where he stays until the birth of their first child.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:I_165-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:I-165">[154]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_80">3E 80</span></h4>
<p><i>The Wolf Queen</i> mentions the following rulers:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Daggerfall" title="Daggerfall">Daggerfall</a>: Ruled by <a href="/wiki/Mortyn" title="Mortyn">Mortyn</a>, son of <a href="/wiki/Gothlyr" title="Gothlyr">Gothlyr</a>.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Silvenar" title="Silvenar">Silvenar</a>: Position held by <a href="/wiki/Varbarenth" title="Varbarenth">Varbarenth</a>, son of <a href="/wiki/Varbaril?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Varbaril (page does not exist)">Varbaril</a>.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Lilmoth" title="Lilmoth">Lilmoth</a>: <a href="/wiki/Lady_Ioa" title="Lady Ioa" class="mw-redirect">Lady Ioa</a> rules this. Normally, the position is ruled by a Warlord.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:I_165-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:I-165">[154]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_81">3E 81</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Potema_Septim" title="Potema Septim">Potema Septim</a> (then 14), daughter of <a href="/wiki/Pelagius_Septim_II" title="Pelagius Septim II">Pelagius Septim II</a>, and granddaughter of current emperor <a href="/wiki/Uriel_Septim_II" title="Uriel Septim II">Uriel Septim II</a>, marries the 62-year-old <a href="/wiki/Nord" title="Nord">Nordic</a> King of <a href="/wiki/Solitude" title="Solitude">Solitude</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mantiarco" title="Mantiarco">Mantiarco</a>, in an arranged marriage.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:II_167-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:II-167">[156]</a></sup>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_99">3E 99</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Antiochus_Septim" title="Antiochus Septim">Antiochus Septim</a> is crowned <a href="/wiki/Emperor" title="Emperor">Emperor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BHoE:I_151-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BHoE:I-151">[142]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Quintilla" title="Quintilla">Quintilla</a> dies, with her only regret "being that she will not live to see <a href="/wiki/Uriel_Septim_III" title="Uriel Septim III">Uriel Septim III</a> be crowned as King of <a href="/wiki/Solitude" title="Solitude">Solitude</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:III_166-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:III-166">[155]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Potema_Septim" title="Potema Septim">Potema Septim</a> tries to blackmail <a href="/wiki/Antiochus_Septim" title="Antiochus Septim">Antiochus Septim</a> into not accepting the position of Emperor. Learning from the mistakes of the past, he instead produces evidence of his own, showing a forgery of hers to clear the way for her son to be King of Solitude, and she withdraws her attempts.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:III_166-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:III-166">[155]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2nd_Century_3">2nd Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_100">3E 100</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Nordic King <a href="/wiki/Mantiarco" title="Mantiarco">Mantiarco</a> of <a href="/wiki/Solitude" title="Solitude">Solitude</a> dies, as predicted by the sorceress and Dowager Empress <a href="/wiki/Quintilla" title="Quintilla">Quintilla</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:III_166-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:III-166">[155]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_104">3E 104</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Antiochus_Septim" title="Antiochus Septim">Antiochus Septim</a> has a daughter to his second wife, <a href="/wiki/Gysilla" title="Gysilla">Gysilla</a>, whom he names <a href="/wiki/Kintyra_II" title="Kintyra II" class="mw-redirect">Kintyra</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:IV_168-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:IV-168">[157]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_105">3E 105</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/University_of_Gwylim" title="University of Gwylim">University of Gwylim</a> translates "Opusculus Lamae Bal ta Mezzamortie" (A brief account of Lamae Bal and the Restless Death).<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">[158]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_109">3E 109</span></h4>
<ul><li>Antiochus continues to mismanage the Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:IV_168-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:IV-168">[157]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Magnus_Septim" title="Magnus Septim">Magnus Septim</a> is now married to Cyrodiil Queen Hellena, and both are suitably managing the affairs of the <a href="/wiki/Black_Marsh" title="Black Marsh">Black Marsh</a>, from <a href="/wiki/Lilmoth" title="Lilmoth">Lilmoth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:IV_168-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:IV-168">[157]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Cephorus_Septim" title="Cephorus Septim">Cephorus Septim</a> and his wife Bianki were ruling the <a href="/wiki/Hammerfell" title="Hammerfell">Hammerfell</a> Kingdom of <a href="/wiki/Gilane" title="Gilane">Gilane</a> with a healthy brood of children.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:IV_168-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:IV-168">[157]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Potema_Septim" title="Potema Septim">Potema Septim</a> makes negotiations with the <a href="/wiki/Psijic_Order" title="Psijic Order">Psijic Order</a> to deal with the upcoming <a href="/wiki/Pyandonea" title="Pyandonea">Pyandonean</a> attack of <a href="/wiki/Tamriel" title="Tamriel">Tamriel</a>, negotiating a deal for their help for eight million gold.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:IV_168-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:IV-168">[157]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_110">3E 110</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Isle" title="War of the Isle">War of the Isle</a> takes place between the <a href="/wiki/Altmer" title="Altmer">Altmer</a> of <a href="/wiki/Summerset_Isles" title="Summerset Isles">Summerset Isles</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Maormer" title="Maormer">Maormer</a> of <a href="/wiki/Pyandonea" title="Pyandonea">Pyandonea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:V_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:V-3">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:P_123-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:P-123">[117]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BHoE:I_151-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BHoE:I-151">[142]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TKofN_170-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TKofN-170">[159]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Iachesis" title="Iachesis">Iachesis</a> is still the head of <a href="/wiki/Psijic_Order" title="Psijic Order">Psijic Order</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:IV_168-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:IV-168">[157]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_111">3E 111</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Knights_of_the_Nine_(Faction)" title="Knights of the Nine (Faction)">Knights of the Nine</a> is founded by <a href="/wiki/Sir_Amiel_Lannus" title="Sir Amiel Lannus">Sir Amiel Lannus</a>, after his triumphant return from battle in the <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Isle" title="War of the Isle">War of the Isle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TKofN_170-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TKofN-170">[159]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_119">3E 119</span></h4>
<ul><li>During a rare visitation from his sister <a href="/wiki/Potema_Septim" title="Potema Septim">Potema</a> and nephew <a href="/wiki/Uriel_Septim_III" title="Uriel Septim III">Uriel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Antiochus" title="Antiochus" class="mw-redirect">Antiochus</a>, who had suffered from several illnesses over his reign, lapsed into a coma.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:V_171-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:V-171">[160]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Elder_Council" title="Elder Council">Elder Council</a> prepares for the ascension of Antiochus' fifteen-year-old daughter, <a href="/wiki/Kintyra_II" title="Kintyra II" class="mw-redirect">Kintyra</a>, to take the throne.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:V_171-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:V-171">[160]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Pelagius_Septim_III" title="Pelagius Septim III">Pelagius Septim III</a> is born in <a href="/wiki/Wayrest" title="Wayrest">Wayrest</a>, son of <a href="/wiki/Magnus_Septim" title="Magnus Septim">Magnus Septim</a> and his wife Hellena.<sup id="cite_ref-MoP_172-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MoP-172">[161]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_120">3E 120</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Kintyra_II" title="Kintyra II" class="mw-redirect">Kintyra II</a> becomes the next Empress of the Septim Dynasty.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:VI_173-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:VI-173">[162]</a></sup>
</li><li>Queen <a href="/wiki/Potema_Septim" title="Potema Septim">Potema Septim</a> gathers her forces for the rebellion against the Empire, for what will later be called the <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Red_Diamond" title="War of the Red Diamond">War of the Red Diamond</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:V_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:V-3">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceB_53-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceB-53">[52]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:V_171-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:V-171">[160]</a></sup>
</li><li>Some sources claim that the War of the Red Diamond began in this year.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_121">3E 121</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Kintyra_II" title="Kintyra II" class="mw-redirect">Kintyra II</a> is captured by <a href="/wiki/Potema_Septim" title="Potema Septim">Queen Potema</a>'s forces. <a href="/wiki/Uriel_Septim_III" title="Uriel Septim III">Uriel Septim III</a> proclaims himself as the new Emperor of Tamriel.<sup id="cite_ref-BHoE:I_151-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BHoE:I-151">[142]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:VI_173-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:VI-173">[162]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Red_Diamond" title="War of the Red Diamond">War of the Red Diamond</a> begins.<sup id="cite_ref-BHoE:I_151-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BHoE:I-151">[142]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TKofN_170-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TKofN-170">[159]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_123">3E 123</span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_125">3E 125</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Cephorus_Septim" title="Cephorus Septim">Cephorus Septim</a> reconquers the western half of the <a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a> region.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:VII_175-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:VII-175">[164]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_127">3E 127</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Ichidag" title="Battle of Ichidag">Battle of Ichidag</a> takes place – <a href="/wiki/Uriel_Septim_III" title="Uriel Septim III">Uriel Septim III</a> and his forces fight against <a href="/wiki/Cephorus_Septim" title="Cephorus Septim">Cephorus Septim</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hammerfell" title="Hammerfell">Hammerfell</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BotWQ_164-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BotWQ-164">[153]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:VII_175-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:VII-175">[164]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:VIII_176-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:VIII-176">[165]</a></sup>
</li><li>During this battle, <a href="/wiki/Uriel_Septim_III" title="Uriel Septim III">Uriel Septim III</a> is captured by <a href="/wiki/Cephorus_Septim" title="Cephorus Septim">Cephorus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:VIII_176-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:VIII-176">[165]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BHoE:II_177-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BHoE:II-177">[166]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Falconstar" title="Battle of Falconstar">Battle of Falconstar</a> – <a href="/wiki/Potema_Septim" title="Potema Septim">Queen Potema</a> fights against <a href="/wiki/Magnus_Septim" title="Magnus Septim">Magnus Septim</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BotWQ_164-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BotWQ-164">[153]</a></sup>
</li><li>En route to his trial in the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_City" title="Imperial City">Imperial City</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uriel_Septim_III" title="Uriel Septim III">Uriel Septim III</a> is burned alive inside his prisoner's carriage by an angry mob. <a href="/wiki/Cephorus_Septim" title="Cephorus Septim">Cephorus Septim</a> is proclaimed Emperor.<sup id="cite_ref-BHoE:II_177-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BHoE:II-177">[166]</a></sup>
</li><li>In return for their pledges of allegiance to the Empire, the nobility of <a href="/wiki/Skyrim" title="Skyrim">Skyrim</a>, <a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hammerfell" title="Hammerfell">Hammerfell</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Summerset_Isle" title="Summerset Isle" class="mw-redirect">Summerset Isle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Valenwood" title="Valenwood">Valenwood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Black_Marsh" title="Black Marsh">Black Marsh</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Morrowind" title="Morrowind">Morrowind</a> demanded and received a new level of autonomy and independence from the Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-TWQ:VIII_176-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TWQ:VIII-176">[165]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Red_Diamond" title="War of the Red Diamond">War of the Red Diamond</a> ends, and <a href="/wiki/Cephorus_Septim" title="Cephorus Septim">Cephorus Septim</a> becomes Emperor.<sup id="cite_ref-TDC_10-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TDC-10">[11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_246">3E 246</span></h4>

The reason for this was to discourage absent and foreign landlords.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">[171]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_267">3E 267</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Firewaves" title="Battle of Firewaves">Battle of Firewaves</a> occurs in and around <a href="/wiki/Dwynnen" title="Dwynnen">Dwynnen</a>, despite it not having a sea port.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:V_3-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:V-3">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FotU_186-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FotU-186">[174]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/High_Rock" title="High Rock">High Rock</a> actually begins building defenses against the <a href="/wiki/Camoran_Usurper" title="Camoran Usurper">Camoran Usurper</a>. The reason for the delay was that the "primary powers of the Bay were ruled by particularly inept monarchs - <a href="/wiki/Wayrest" title="Wayrest">Wayrest</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sentinel" title="Sentinel">Sentinel</a> both had kings in their minority (EDITOR: Children), and <a href="/wiki/Daggerfall" title="Daggerfall">Daggerfall</a> was torn by contention between Helena and her cousin Jilathe. The Lord of Reich Gradkeep (now <a href="/wiki/Anticlere" title="Anticlere">Anticlere</a>) was deathly ill through 266 and finally died at the end of the year. There were, in short, no leaders to unite the province against the Usurper."<sup id="cite_ref-FotU_186-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FotU-186">[174]</a></sup>
</li><li>Eight separate, minor landowners make deals with the Camoran Usurper to allow them to keep their land.<sup id="cite_ref-FotU_186-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FotU-186">[174]</a></sup>
</li><li>The reign of the Camoran Usurper is ended.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:Eras_2-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:Eras-2">[3]</a></sup>
</li></ul>

This is compared with the original population of 211 people.<sup id="cite_ref-AHoD_1-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AHoD-1">[2]</a></sup>

This is an example of a <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Break" title="Dragon Break">Dragon Break</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:O_63-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:O-63">[62]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:F_157-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:F-157">[146]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">[200]</a></sup>

</li><li>The Telvanni Council objects to the injunctions being placed on the slave trade, which it claims are "guaranteed by the terms of the Treaty of the Armistics, and Telvanni Council will not entertain any discussions of abridgments of those rights."<sup id="cite_ref-PGE3:M_19-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PGE3:M-19">[20]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BB426_217-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BB426-217">[204]</a></sup>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_427">3E 427</span></h4>
<ul><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_III:_Morrowind" title="The Elder Scrolls III: Morrowind">The Elder Scrolls III: Morrowind</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:M_221-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:M-221">[208]</a></sup>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Nerevarine" title="Nerevarine">Nerevarine</a> is discovered, and at the same time the <a href="/wiki/Nerevarine_Prophecy" title="Nerevarine Prophecy">Prophecy of the Nerevarine</a> is revealed to be true.
</li><li>The Nerevarine reclaimed the <a href="/wiki/Moon-and-Star" title="Moon-and-Star">Moon-and-Star</a> from <a href="/wiki/Azura" title="Azura">Azura</a>, proving himself to be the true Incarnate of <a href="/wiki/Nerevar" title="Nerevar" class="mw-redirect">Nerevar</a>.
</li><li>The Nerevarine became the <a href="/wiki/Hortator" title="Hortator">Hortator</a> and united all three <a href="/wiki/Great_House" title="Great House" class="mw-redirect">Great Houses</a> to oppose <a href="/wiki/Dagoth_Ur_(Character)" title="Dagoth Ur (Character)">Dagoth Ur</a>.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Dagoth_Ur_(Character)" title="Dagoth Ur (Character)">Dagoth Ur</a> is killed at <a href="/wiki/Red_Mountain" title="Red Mountain">Red Mountain</a> by the Nerevarine.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:M_221-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:M-221">[208]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
</li><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_III:_Tribunal" title="The Elder Scrolls III: Tribunal">The Elder Scrolls III: Tribunal</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:T_222-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:T-222">[209]</a></sup>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Nerevarine" title="Nerevarine">Nerevarine</a> reclaimed <a href="/wiki/Trueflame" title="Trueflame">Trueflame</a> as his weapon.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Sotha_Sil" title="Sotha Sil">Sotha Sil</a> is betrayed and killed by <a href="/wiki/Almalexia_(God)" title="Almalexia (God)" class="mw-redirect">Almalexia</a> who is then killed by the <a href="/wiki/Nerevarine" title="Nerevarine">Nerevarine</a> in self-defense.
</li></ul>
</li><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_III:_Bloodmoon" title="The Elder Scrolls III: Bloodmoon">The Elder Scrolls III: Bloodmoon</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:B_223-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:B-223">[210]</a></sup>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Nerevarine" title="Nerevarine">Nerevarine</a> is named a <a href="/wiki/Blodskaal" title="Blodskaal">Blodskaal</a> (Bloodbrother) of the <a href="/wiki/Skaal_Village_(Bloodmoon)" title="Skaal Village (Bloodmoon)">Skaal Village</a> on <a href="/wiki/Solstheim_(Bloodmoon)" title="Solstheim (Bloodmoon)">Solstheim</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:B_223-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:B-223">[210]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Nerevarine defeats <a href="/wiki/Hircine" title="Hircine">Hircine</a><sup id="cite_ref-TES:B_223-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:B-223">[210]</a></sup> and stops the <a href="/wiki/Bloodmoon_Prophecy" title="Bloodmoon Prophecy" class="mw-redirect">Bloodmoon Prophecy</a> from being fulfilled.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:B_223-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:B-223">[210]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Raven_Rock_(Bloodmoon)" title="Raven Rock (Bloodmoon)">Raven Rock</a> is founded.
</li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_431">3E 431</span></h4>
<ul><li>An Addendum is added to the Mages Guild charter: <i>"Any guild member commiting a crime against the Guild is to be suspended immediately. The suspension may be lifted at the discretion of the Steward of the Council of Mages. Any guild member receiving multiple suspensions may, at the determination of the council, be summarily and permanently dismissed from the guild."</i><sup id="cite_ref-MGC_101-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MGC-101">[95]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Mages_Guild" title="Mages Guild">Mages Guild</a> Charter changed by Arch-Mage <a href="/wiki/Hannibal_Traven" title="Hannibal Traven">Hannibal Traven</a> to include a provision that all candidates for membership of the Mages Guild must first gain acceptance from all the Guild Hall stewards.<sup id="cite_ref-MGC_101-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MGC-101">[95]</a></sup>
</li><li>Mages Guild distributes the schools of magic to different Guild Halls. For instance, Alteration is taught at <a href="/wiki/Cheydinhal_(Oblivion)" title="Cheydinhal (Oblivion)">Cheydinhal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-MGC_101-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MGC-101">[95]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Farwil" title="Farwil" class="mw-redirect">Farwil</a>, son of Cheydinhal's <a href="/wiki/Count_Andel_Indarys" title="Count Andel Indarys" class="mw-redirect">Count Andel Indarys</a>, forms the <a href="/wiki/Knights_of_the_Thorn" title="Knights of the Thorn">Knights of the Thorn</a>.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Wiki:Sourcing" title="The Elder Scrolls Wiki:Sourcing"><i>source?</i></a>&#93;</sup>
</li><li>The events taking place in <i><a href="/wiki/Grommok%27s_Journal" title="Grommok's Journal">Grommok's Journal</a></i> occur in this year.<sup id="cite_ref-GromJournal_224-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GromJournal-224">[211]</a></sup>
<ul><li>12th of <a href="/wiki/Rain%27s_Hand" title="Rain's Hand" class="mw-redirect">Rain's Hand</a>: Grommok, Lewin, and Syndelius explore <a href="/wiki/Fort_Wariel" title="Fort Wariel">Fort Wariel</a>, after which they travel north to the <a href="/wiki/Ayleid_Ruin" title="Ayleid Ruin" class="mw-redirect">Ayleid Ruin</a> of <a href="/wiki/Trumbe" title="Trumbe">Trumbe</a> and discover a locked box that they cannot open easily.<sup id="cite_ref-GromJournal_224-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GromJournal-224">[211]</a></sup>
</li><li>13th of Rain's Hand: After opening the cask, they discover an <a href="/wiki/Akaviri" title="Akaviri">Akaviri</a> sword which they name "<a href="/wiki/Dawnfang" title="Dawnfang" class="mw-redirect">Dawnfang</a>" and "<a href="/wiki/Duskfang" title="Duskfang" class="mw-redirect">Duskfang</a>," on account of its varying colors at different times. Grommok claims the sword for his own.<sup id="cite_ref-GromJournal_224-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GromJournal-224">[211]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
</li></ul>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="3E_433">3E 433</span></h4>
<ul><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_IV:_Oblivion" title="The Elder Scrolls IV: Oblivion">The Elder Scrolls IV: Oblivion</a></i> take place during this year.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:O_226-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:O-226">[212]</a></sup>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Oblivion_Crisis" title="Oblivion Crisis">Oblivion Crisis</a> occurs.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:O_226-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:O-226">[212]</a></sup>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Uriel_Septim_VII" title="Uriel Septim VII">Uriel Septim VII</a> is killed by a <a href="/wiki/Mythic_Dawn" title="Mythic Dawn">Mythic Dawn</a> agent.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:O_226-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:O-226">[212]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">[213]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Hero_of_Kvatch" title="Hero of Kvatch">A new hero</a> stands up and greatly aids the Septim dynasty and the <a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Tamriel" title="Empire of Tamriel" class="mw-redirect">Empire</a>.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Martin_Septim" title="Martin Septim">Martin Septim</a> is crowned as the Emperor.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:O_226-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:O-226">[212]</a></sup>
</li><li>Martin Septim sacrifices himself in the <a href="/wiki/Imperial_City" title="Imperial City">Imperial City</a> to banish <a href="/wiki/Mehrunes_Dagon" title="Mehrunes Dagon">Mehrunes Dagon</a> from <a href="/wiki/Nirn" title="Nirn">Nirn</a> and save the people of the Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:O_226-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:O-226">[212]</a></sup>
</li><li>Martin Septim's death ends the <a href="/wiki/Third_Era" title="Third Era">Third Era</a> and begins the <a href="/wiki/Fourth_Era" title="Fourth Era">Fourth</a>.
</li><li>End of the <a href="/wiki/Septim_Dynasty" title="Septim Dynasty">Septim Dynasty</a>; destruction of the <a href="/wiki/Amulet_of_Kings" title="Amulet of Kings">Amulet of Kings</a>.
</li></ul>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Attack_on_the_Mages_Guild" title="Attack on the Mages Guild" class="mw-redirect">Attack on the Mages Guild</a>. The Necromancer <a href="/wiki/Mannimarco" title="Mannimarco">Mannimarco</a> wages war on the Mages Guild, almost succeeding before being killed by the new <a href="/wiki/Hero_of_Kvatch" title="Hero of Kvatch">High Wizard</a>.
</li><li>An <a href="/wiki/Elder_Scroll_(Lore)" title="Elder Scroll (Lore)" class="mw-redirect">Elder Scroll</a> is successfully stolen from <a href="/wiki/White-Gold_Tower" title="White-Gold Tower">White-Gold Tower</a> by a member of the <a href="/wiki/Thieves_Guild" title="Thieves Guild">Thieves Guild</a>.
</li></ul>
</li><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_IV:_Knights_of_the_Nine" title="The Elder Scrolls IV: Knights of the Nine">The Elder Scrolls IV: Knights of the Nine</a></i> take place.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Auroran_Crisis" title="Auroran Crisis">Auroran Crisis</a> occurs.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:SI_228-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:SI-228">[214]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Hero_of_Kvatch" title="Hero of Kvatch">Hero of Kvatch</a> becomes the 2nd Divine Crusader and defeats <a href="/wiki/Umaril_the_Unfeathered" title="Umaril the Unfeathered" class="mw-redirect">Umaril</a> both in the mortal and spiritual planes.
</li></ul>
</li><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_IV:_Shivering_Isles" title="The Elder Scrolls IV: Shivering Isles">The Elder Scrolls IV: Shivering Isles</a></i> take place.
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Greymarch_(Shivering_Isles)" title="Greymarch (Shivering Isles)" class="mw-redirect">Greymarch</a> occurs once again.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:SI_228-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:SI-228">[214]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Hero of Kvatch is crowned as the new Sheogorath and defeats <a href="/wiki/Jyggalag" title="Jyggalag">Jyggalag</a>.
</li></ul>
</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_Era">Fourth Era</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1st_Century_5">1st Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_0">4E 0</span></h4>
<ul><li>A new era begins after the <a href="/wiki/Oblivion_Crisis" title="Oblivion Crisis">Oblivion Crisis</a> comes to an end.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:O_226-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:O-226">[212]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/High_Chancellor_Ocato" title="High Chancellor Ocato" class="mw-redirect">High Chancellor Ocato</a> unsuccessfully attempts to bring the Empire a new Emperor after the Oblivion Crisis.<sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">[215]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_02">4E 02</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Sinderion" title="Sinderion">Sinderion</a> delivers a speech to the <a href="/wiki/Alchemical_Symposium" title="Alchemical Symposium">Alchemical Symposium</a> about <a href="/wiki/Nirnroot" title="Nirnroot">Nirnroot</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-nirnroot_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nirnroot-44">[43]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_05">4E 05</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Baar_Dau" title="Baar Dau" class="mw-redirect">Baar Dau</a> falls from the sky due to the disappearance of <a href="/wiki/Vivec" title="Vivec">Vivec</a>. Causing the complete destruction of <a href="/wiki/Vivec_City" title="Vivec City">Vivec City</a>.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Wiki:Sourcing" title="The Elder Scrolls Wiki:Sourcing"><i>source?</i></a>&#93;</sup>
</li><li>Red Mountain erupts and the <a href="/wiki/Red_Year" title="Red Year">Red Year</a> begins.<sup id="cite_ref-LTJ_230-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LTJ-230">[216]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-LoS_231-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LoS-231">[OOG 10]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_06">4E 06</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Argonian invasion of southern Morrowind begins.<sup id="cite_ref-LTJ_230-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LTJ-230">[216]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_10">4E 10</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/High_Chancellor_Ocato" title="High Chancellor Ocato" class="mw-redirect">High Chancellor Ocato</a> is killed, most likely by the Thalmor.<sup id="cite_ref-RTIV_232-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RTIV-232">[217]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_16">4E 16</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/High_King" title="High King">High King</a> of <a href="/wiki/Skyrim" title="Skyrim">Skyrim</a> gives <a href="/wiki/Solstheim" title="Solstheim">Solstheim</a> to the Dunmer as a result of the <a href="/wiki/Red_Year" title="Red Year">Red Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-LoS_231-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LoS-231">[OOG 10]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_17">4E 17</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Titus_Mede_I" title="Titus Mede I">Titus Mede I</a> ascends to the throne of Emperor around this time.<sup id="cite_ref-RTIV_232-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RTIV-232">[217]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_20">4E 20</span></h4>
<ul><li>Dunmer refugees use the <a href="/wiki/Dunmeth_Pass" title="Dunmeth Pass">Dunmeth Pass</a> to travel into Skyrim, and <a href="/wiki/Refugees%27_Rest" title="Refugees' Rest">Refugees' Rest</a> is decreed to be a monument.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">[218]</a></sup>
</li><li><i><a href="/wiki/The_Armorer%27s_Challenge" title="The Armorer's Challenge">The Armorer's Challenge</a></i> is written.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">[219]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_22">4E 22</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Thalmor_(Skyrim)" title="Thalmor (Skyrim)">Thalmor</a> came into power of <a href="/wiki/Summerset_Isle" title="Summerset Isle" class="mw-redirect">Summerset Isle</a>. Summerset Isle is renamed to <a href="/wiki/Alinor" title="Alinor">Alinor</a>, but is still referred to as Summerset Isle outside the <a href="/wiki/Third_Aldmeri_Dominion" title="Third Aldmeri Dominion" class="mw-redirect">Third Aldmeri Dominion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_29">4E 29</span></h4>
<ul><li>The government of <a href="/wiki/Valenwood" title="Valenwood">Valenwood</a> is overthrown by the Thalmor sympathizers. The <a href="/wiki/Bosmer" title="Bosmer">Bosmeri</a>, allied with the Empire, were unprepared. Valenwood becomes a Thalmor territory.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Third Aldmeri Dominion severs all ties with the Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_38">4E 38</span></h4>
<ul><li>A great warrior from <a href="/wiki/Windhelm_(Skyrim)" title="Windhelm (Skyrim)">Windhelm</a>, Vundheim, dies. His son, Deroct, lights a candle above the hearth in his home in his honor. The building later becomes known as <a href="/wiki/Candlehearth_Hall" title="Candlehearth Hall">Candlehearth Hall</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">[221]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_42">4E 42</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Night_of_Green_Fire" title="Night of Green Fire">Night of Green Fire</a> occurs. Altmer dissidents fleeing the Dominion are massacred by Thalmor agents in Sentinel.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">[222]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_49">4E 49</span></h4>
<ul><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/An_Elder_Scrolls_Novel:_The_Infernal_City" title="An Elder Scrolls Novel: The Infernal City">An Elder Scrolls Novel: The Infernal City</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Infernal_City_238-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Infernal_City-238">[223]</a></sup>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Umbriel" title="Umbriel">Umbriel</a> appears, terrorizing Tamriel, starting with <a href="/wiki/Lilmoth" title="Lilmoth">Lilmoth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-infernal_239-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-infernal-239">[OOG 11]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
</li><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/An_Elder_Scrolls_Novel:_Lord_of_Souls" title="An Elder Scrolls Novel: Lord of Souls">An Elder Scrolls Novel: Lord of Souls</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-Lord_of_Souls_240-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lord_of_Souls-240">[224]</a></sup>
<ul><li>Umbriel <a href="/wiki/Siege_of_the_Imperial_City_(4E_49)" title="Siege of the Imperial City (4E 49)">besieges</a> the Imperial City, but is stopped before Vuhon can emancipate the city from Oblivion.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_Wiki:Sourcing" title="The Elder Scrolls Wiki:Sourcing"><i>source?</i></a>&#93;</sup>
</li></ul>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_58">4E 58</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Sinderion" title="Sinderion">Sinderion</a> records his findings about <a href="/wiki/Nirnroot" title="Nirnroot">nirnroot</a> in his <a href="/wiki/Sinderion%27s_Field_Journal" title="Sinderion's Field Journal">journal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">[225]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_65">4E 65</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/House_Redoran" title="House Redoran">House Redoran</a> Councillor <a href="/wiki/Brara_Morvayn" title="Brara Morvayn" class="mw-redirect">Brara Morvayn</a> dies.<sup id="cite_ref-RR2_242-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RR2-242">[226]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Lleril_Morvayn" title="Lleril Morvayn">Lleril Morvayn</a> becomes councillor.<sup id="cite_ref-RR2_242-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RR2-242">[226]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_95">4E 95</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/House_Hlaalu" title="House Hlaalu">House Hlaalu</a> member, <a href="/wiki/Vilur_Ulen" title="Vilur Ulen">Vilur Ulen</a> attempts to assassinate <a href="/wiki/Lleril_Morvayn" title="Lleril Morvayn">Lleril Morvayn</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-RR3_243-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RR3-243">[227]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_98">4E 98</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Void_Nights" title="Void Nights">Void Nights</a> begin.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_99">4E 99</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Third_Aldmeri_Dominion" title="Third Aldmeri Dominion" class="mw-redirect">Third Aldmeri Dominion</a> ceases their 70 year-long period of isolation from the Empire.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_100">4E 100</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Void_Nights" title="Void Nights">Void Nights</a> end.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2nd_Century_4">2nd Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_115">4E 115</span></h4>
<ul><li>Coup against the <a href="/wiki/Elsweyr_Confederacy" title="Elsweyr Confederacy">Elsweyr Confederacy</a> takes place. <a href="/wiki/Elsweyr" title="Elsweyr">Elsweyr</a> is divided into the kingdoms of <a href="/wiki/Anequina" title="Anequina">Anequina</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pelletine" title="Pelletine">Pelletine</a>, as extensions of the <a href="/wiki/Aldmeri_Dominion_(Skyrim)" title="Aldmeri Dominion (Skyrim)">Aldmeri Dominion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_122">4E 122</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/The_Great_Collapse" title="The Great Collapse">The Great Collapse</a> of <a href="/wiki/Winterhold_(City)" title="Winterhold (City)">Winterhold</a> occurs.<sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">[228]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_129">4E 129</span></h4>
<ul><li>The people of <a href="/wiki/Riften" title="Riften">Riften</a> overwhelm the city guard and kill <a href="/wiki/Hosgunn_Crossed-Daggers" title="Hosgunn Crossed-Daggers">Hosgunn Crossed-Daggers</a>, the "black-hearted" <a href="/wiki/Jarl" title="Jarl">Jarl</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">[229]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_130">4E 130</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/The_Bulwark" title="The Bulwark">The Bulwark</a> shows signs of crumbling.<sup id="cite_ref-RR3_243-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RR3-243">[227]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_150">4E 150</span></h4>
<ul><li>A small force of Argonians arrives on Solstheim to wreak havoc, but is repelled by Lleril Morvayn.<sup id="cite_ref-RR3_243-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RR3-243">[227]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_168">4E 168</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Titus_Mede_II" title="Titus Mede II">Titus Mede II</a> is crowned <a href="/wiki/Emperor" title="Emperor">Emperor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_170">4E 170</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Raven_Rock" title="Raven Rock">Raven Rock</a> Ebony Mine shows signs of beginning to dry up.<sup id="cite_ref-RR3_243-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RR3-243">[227]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_171">4E 171</span></h4>
<ul><li>The Ambassador of the <a href="/wiki/Aldmeri_Dominion_(Skyrim)" title="Aldmeri Dominion (Skyrim)">Aldmeri Dominion</a> orders the Empire to step down from power. The Empire resists, and the <a href="/wiki/Great_War" title="Great War">Great War</a> between <a href="/wiki/Empire" title="Empire" class="mw-redirect">The Empire</a> and the Aldmeri Dominion begins.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>Aldmeri forces led by Lord Naarifin invade <a href="/wiki/Hammerfell" title="Hammerfell">Hammerfell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cyrodiil" title="Cyrodiil">Cyrodiil</a>. The city of Leyawiin falls, and the city of Bravil is besieged.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>A 2nd <a href="/wiki/Aldmer" title="Aldmer">Aldmeri</a> force, led by Lady Arannelya, cross western Cyrodiil and invade Hammerfell. The <a href="/wiki/Redguard" title="Redguard">Redguards</a> in Hammerfell, divided by civil war and disorganized, put up little resistance. The southern coastline falls to the Aldmeri forces as the Imperial Legions in Hammerfell retreat North into the <a href="/wiki/Alik%27r_Desert" title="Alik'r Desert">Alik'r Desert</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/March_of_Thirst" title="March of Thirst">March of Thirst</a> occurs.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_172">4E 172</span></h4>
<ul><li>Aldmeri forces advance into Cyrodiil to capture the Imperial City.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>Cyrodiil: The cities of Bravil and Anvil in Cyrodiil both fall to Aldmeri forces. Naval battles ensues in Lake Rumare surrounding Imperial City and along the Niben River leading to the Rumare.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>Hammerfell: The entire southern coastline falls to the Aldmeri forces with the exception of Helgathe.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_173">4E 173</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Cyrodiil" title="Cyrodiil">Cyrodiil</a>: Aldmeri forces cross the <a href="/wiki/Niben_River" title="Niben River">Niben</a> and advance towards the Imperial City through the eastern bank, surrounding the city from the east, south, and west.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Hammerfell" title="Hammerfell">Hammerfell</a>: The siege of <a href="/wiki/Hegathe" title="Hegathe">Hegathe</a> is broken. Imperial forces make a stand in <a href="/wiki/Skaven" title="Skaven" class="mw-redirect">Skaven</a> to fight off the advancing Aldmeri soldiers. Skaven falls to the Aldmeri. However, the victorious Aldmeri force is severely weakened by the advance through the desert, and is unable to continue their campaign.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_174">4E 174</span></h4>
<ul><li>Cyrodiil: The Thalmor leadership decides to focus their forces in the Cyrodiil campaign.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>Imperial City falls to the Aldmeri forces.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/The_Reach" title="The Reach">The Reach</a> and <a href="/wiki/Markarth" title="Markarth">Markarth</a> falls to the <a href="/wiki/Reachmen" title="Reachmen">Reachmen</a> in The Forsworn Uprising and is ruled as an independent kingdom.<sup id="cite_ref-bear_246-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bear-246">[230]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_175">4E 175</span></h4>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Red_Ring" title="Battle of the Red Ring">Battle of the Red Ring</a> takes place as the Empire embarks on a campaign to retake Imperial City, which fell to the Aldmeri Dominion the previous year. The battle was an Imperial victory, but not without heavy losses.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>Exhausted from war, the Empire negotiates a peace treaty and signs the <a href="/wiki/White-Gold_Concordat" title="White-Gold Concordat">White-Gold Concordat</a> with the Aldmeri Dominion, thus ending the war. The terms of the agreements are the surrender of the remaining territory still occupied by Aldmeri Force, and the banning of the worship of <a href="/wiki/Talos" title="Talos">Talos</a>. Thus, the <a href="/wiki/Great_War" title="Great War">Great War</a> ends.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>As a result of the White-Gold Concordat, relationship between the Imperials of Cyrodiil and the <a href="/wiki/Redguard" title="Redguard">Redguard</a> of <a href="/wiki/Hammerfell" title="Hammerfell">Hammerfell</a> deteriorated. Although allies during the war, the Empire is forced to renounce Hammerfell as an Imperial province.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li><li>All the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Scroll_(Lore)" title="Elder Scroll (Lore)" class="mw-redirect">Elder Scrolls</a> housed in the libraries of <a href="/wiki/White-Gold_Tower" title="White-Gold Tower">White-Gold Tower</a> vanish, and are scattered across Tamriel by unknown means.<sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247">[231]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_176">4E 176</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ulfric_Stormcloak" title="Ulfric Stormcloak">Ulfric Stormcloak</a> and his militia retake <a href="/wiki/The_Reach" title="The Reach">The Reach</a> and <a href="/wiki/Markarth" title="Markarth">Markarth</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Reachmen" title="Reachmen">Reachmen</a>. The surviving Reachmen flee to the hills of the Reach and became known as the Forsworn, a clan commonly known to hold a bitter hatred for Nords.<sup id="cite_ref-bear_246-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bear-246">[230]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Stormcloaks are founded.<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248">[232]</a></sup>
<ul><li>Somewhere between 4E 176 and 4E 199 the <a href="/wiki/Skyrim_Civil_War" title="Skyrim Civil War">Skyrim Civil War</a> breaks out.<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">[233]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250">[234]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_180">4E 180</span></h4>
<ul><li>As a follow-up to the <a href="/wiki/White-Gold_Concordat" title="White-Gold Concordat">White-Gold Concordat</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Second_Treaty_of_Stros_M%27kai" title="Second Treaty of Stros M'kai">Second Treaty of Stros M'kai</a> is signed, which results in the Aldmeri forces withdrawing from Hammerfell.<sup id="cite_ref-greatwar_235-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-greatwar-235">[220]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_181">4E 181</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Madanach" title="Madanach">Madanach</a> is captured by <a href="/wiki/Jarl_Igmund" title="Jarl Igmund" class="mw-redirect">Jarl Igmund</a> and imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Cidhna_Mine" title="Cidhna Mine">Cidhna Mine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251">[235]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Raven_Rock" title="Raven Rock">Raven Rock</a>'s Ebony Mine completely dries up.<sup id="cite_ref-RR3_243-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RR3-243">[227]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_186">4E 186</span></h4>

</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_187">4E 187</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Alisanne_Dupre" title="Alisanne Dupre">Alisanne Dupre</a> considers reopening the Black Marsh city of <a href="/wiki/Archon" title="Archon">Archon</a> as a training facility for the <a href="/wiki/Shadowscale" title="Shadowscale">Shadowscales</a>, but never goes through with it.<sup id="cite_ref-CJ1_252-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CJ1-252">[236]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_188">4E 188</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wayrest" title="Wayrest">Wayrest</a> falls to corsairs.<sup id="cite_ref-ciceroii_253-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ciceroii-253">[237]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Dark Brotherhood's <a href="/wiki/Wayrest_Sanctuary" title="Wayrest Sanctuary">Wayrest Sanctuary</a> is destroyed by corsairs, and all assassins within are killed.<sup id="cite_ref-ciceroii_253-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ciceroii-253">[237]</a></sup>
</li><li>The city of Bravil erupts into violence as a result of a war between two skooma traffickers.<sup id="cite_ref-ciceroii_253-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ciceroii-253">[237]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Lucky_Old_Lady" title="Lucky Old Lady">Lucky Old Lady</a> statue is destroyed.<sup id="cite_ref-ciceroii_253-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ciceroii-253">[237]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_189">4E 189</span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Cicero" title="Cicero">Cicero</a> becomes The Keeper of <a href="/wiki/The_Night_Mother" title="The Night Mother" class="mw-redirect">The Night Mother</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-254" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254">[238]</a></sup>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Cheydinhal" title="Cheydinhal">Cheydinhal</a> has erupted into violence and chaos; presumably one among many cities in <a href="/wiki/Cyrodiil" title="Cyrodiil">Cyrodiil</a> that has fallen to chaos.<sup id="cite_ref-255" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-255">[239]</a></sup>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="3rd_Century_4">3rd Century</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_201">4E 201</span></h4>
<ul><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim" title="The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim">The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim</a></i> take place this year.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:S_256-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:S-256">[240]</a></sup>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/General_Tullius_(Skyrim)" title="General Tullius (Skyrim)">General Tullius</a> is sent by <a href="/wiki/Titus_Mede_II" title="Titus Mede II">Titus Mede II</a> to Skyrim to end the <a href="/wiki/Civil_War" title="Civil War" class="mw-redirect">Civil War</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-257" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-257">[241]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">[242]</a></sup>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Imperial_Legion_(Skyrim)" title="Imperial Legion (Skyrim)">Imperial Legion</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Stormcloaks" title="Stormcloaks">Stormcloaks</a> battle for control of <a href="/wiki/Skyrim" title="Skyrim">Skyrim</a>.
</li></ul>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Crisis" title="Dragon Crisis">Dragon Crisis</a> begins.
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Alduin" title="Alduin">Alduin</a> is first spotted since his return on the 17th of <a href="/wiki/Last_Seed" title="Last Seed" class="mw-redirect">Last Seed</a>, first attacking the town of <a href="/wiki/Helgen" title="Helgen">Helgen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">[243]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Last_Dragonborn" title="Last Dragonborn">Last Dragonborn</a> emerges and takes on the task of defeating Alduin and the dragons.<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">[244]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261">[245]</a></sup>
</li><li>Alduin is slain by the Dragonborn during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Tongues" title="Battle of the Tongues" class="mw-redirect">Battle of the Tongues</a> in <a href="/wiki/Sovngarde_(Location)" title="Sovngarde (Location)">Sovngarde</a>.
</li></ul>
</li><li>Civil War ends.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:S_256-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:S-256">[240]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/College_of_Winterhold" title="College of Winterhold">College of Winterhold</a> discovers the <a href="/wiki/Eye_of_Magnus" title="Eye of Magnus">Eye of Magnus</a>, which nearly destroys the city of <a href="/wiki/Winterhold" title="Winterhold">Winterhold</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:S_256-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:S-256">[240]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Infamous <a href="/wiki/Left_Eye_of_the_Falmer" title="Left Eye of the Falmer">Eyes of the Falmer</a> were stolen by the <a href="/wiki/Thieves_Guild_(Skyrim)" title="Thieves Guild (Skyrim)">Thieves Guild</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:S_256-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:S-256">[240]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Dark_Brotherhood_(Skyrim)" title="Dark Brotherhood (Skyrim)">Dark Brotherhood</a> is either <a href="/wiki/Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood!" title="Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!">destroyed</a> by the Dragonborn or the Emperor <a href="/wiki/Titus_Mede_II" title="Titus Mede II">Titus Mede II</a> is assassinated by them.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:S_256-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:S-256">[240]</a></sup>
</li><li>The Harbinger of <a href="/wiki/The_Companions" title="The Companions">The Companions</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kodlak_Whitemane" title="Kodlak Whitemane">Kodlak Whitemane</a> dies.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:S_256-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:S-256">[240]</a></sup>
</li><li>The owner of the <a href="/wiki/The_White_Phial_(Location)" title="The White Phial (Location)">White Phial</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nurelion" title="Nurelion">Nurelion</a> died after the White Phial had been recovered to its <a href="/wiki/Repairing_the_Phial" title="Repairing the Phial">former glory</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-262" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-262">[246]</a></sup>
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Gildergreen" title="Gildergreen">Gildergreen</a> in Whiterun returns to its <a href="/wiki/The_Blessings_of_Nature" title="The Blessings of Nature">former glory</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-263" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-263">[247]</a></sup>
</li></ul>
</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="4E_202"> 4E 202 </span></h4>
<ul><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Dawnguard" title="The Elder Scrolls V: Dawnguard">The Elder Scrolls V: Dawnguard</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:DG_264-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:DG-264">[248]</a></sup>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Volkihar_Clan" title="Volkihar Clan">Volkihar Clan</a>'s plan to fulfill the <a href="/wiki/Tyranny_of_the_Sun" title="Tyranny of the Sun">Tyranny of the Sun</a> begins to take form.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Auriel%27s_Bow_(Dawnguard)" title="Auriel's Bow (Dawnguard)">Auriel's Bow</a> is recovered by the Dragonborn and <a href="/wiki/Serana" title="Serana">Serana</a>.
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Lord_Harkon" title="Lord Harkon" class="mw-redirect">Lord Harkon</a> is slain by the Dragonborn.
</li></ul>
</li><li>The events of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Dragonborn" title="The Elder Scrolls V: Dragonborn">The Elder Scrolls V: Dragonborn</a></i> take place.<sup id="cite_ref-TES:DB_265-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TES:DB-265">[249]</a></sup>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Miraak" title="Miraak">Miraak</a>'s influence takes hold of the inhabitants of the isle of <a href="/wiki/Solstheim_(Dragonborn)" title="Solstheim (Dragonborn)">Solstheim</a>.
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Miraak" title="Miraak">First Dragonborn</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Last_Dragonborn" title="Last Dragonborn">Last Dragonborn</a> battle atop the Summit of <a href="/wiki/Apocrypha" title="Apocrypha">Apocrypha</a>. Miraak is then killed by <a href="/wiki/Hermaeus_Mora" title="Hermaeus Mora">Hermaeus Mora</a> when it becomes clear that the Last Dragonborn would prevail.
</li><li>The <a href="/wiki/Served_Cold" title="Served Cold">plot</a> to kill Councilor <a href="/wiki/Lleril_Morvayn" title="Lleril Morvayn">Lleril Morvayn</a> by House Severin is revealed and subsequently stopped.
</li></ul>
</li></ul>
